### [75] [Solitonic Andreev Spin Qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15502)
*Pablo San-Jose,Elsa Prada*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 提出了一种新型超导自旋量子比特（SASQ），结合了Andreev自旋量子比特和几何自旋量子比特的特点。利用Corbino圆盘结构中的自旋态和磁通量 mismatches，实现了有独特自旋简并度的自旋束缚态。通过相位偏置导致自旋的霍尔态旋转，可能覆盖整个布洛赫球。分析了动态漂移的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自旋量子比特的新型结构，特别是利用自旋轨道耦合和超导效应来提升量子比特的信息存储和计算能力。

Method: 通过结合Andreev束缚态和Corbino结构中的自旋态，引入磁通量 mismatch来产生独特的自旋束缚态。利用自旋轨道耦合和霍尔效应来控制自旋旋转。

Result: 成功实现了一个允许自旋密集覆盖布洛赫球的量子比特，为量子计算提供了新方案。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了自旋量子比特的设计，提供了-dot-可以看到, 大致我可以分析这篇论文的内容。它提出了一个新的自旋量子比特结构，称为溶iton型Andreev自旋量子比特(SASQ)，结合了Andreev自旋量子比特和几何自旋量子比特的特点。使用了Corbino盘结构，这样可以在圆形Josephson结的在环形区域内产生自旋简并态。通过引入一个弱磁通量，使得内盘和外环之间的超导体产生一个位相 getSession mismatch，从而抵消了偶联，产生独特的自旋束缚态类似于Jackiw-Rebbi孤子。这些自旋态被定位在结的周围，可以通过改变超导体之间的相位来控制它们的位置。当施加一个相位偏置时，利用2DEG中的自旋轨道耦合，自旋会发生霍尔态的旋转。这样的旋转可以在孤子绕结旋转时，让量子比特在布洛赫球上密集覆盖。还分析了非霍尔态漂移的影响。因此，这种结构利用自旋和超导效应，展现出一种高效的信息存储和计算能力的量子比特新方案。可能需要进一步验证其在实际超导体中的稳定性和动态特性。

Abstract: We propose a novel type of superconducting spin qubit, dubbed solitonic
Andreev spin qubit (SASQ), that combines features of Andreev spin qubits and
geometric spin qubits. The two SASQ states are the degenerate spin orientations
of an Andreev bound state trapped in a circular Josephson junction with a
Corbino disk geometry, created on a 2DEG. The junction is subjected to a weak
magnetic flux that induces a fluxoid mismatch between the inner disk and outer
ring superconductors. The fluxoid mismatch produces a cancellation of the
induced pairing that traps unconventional spin-degenerate Andreev bound states
analogous to Jackiw-Rebbi solitons. They are localized at a position around the
junction that can be controlled by changing the superconducting phase
difference. Moving a soliton with a phase bias induces a holonomic rotation of
its spin, by virtue of the spin-orbit coupling in the 2DEG. The holonomic qubit
trajectories can densely cover the full Bloch sphere as the soliton revolves
around the junction. Effects of non-holonomic (dynamic) qubit drift are also
analyzed.

### [76] [Quantum metric and localization in a quasicrystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15575)
*Quentin Marsal,Patric Holmvall,Annica M. Black-Schaffer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究使用量子度量分析了一维斐波那契准晶体的性质，揭示了量子度量如何关联本地化特征和缩放不变性，提出新定义的度量，揭示了本地化与分形能谱的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过量子度量深入理解准晶体的本地化特性和其尺度不变性，可能会对准晶体学和复杂系统领域产生积极影响。

Method: 该研究利用了量子度量，结合位置和声子组件的Chern数来分析一维斐波那契链的本地化特征，提出了新的度量定义。

Result: 研究发现，量子度量能够更敏感地反映准晶体的本地化特性，引入了新的声子组件和一个混合的声子-位置Chern数，并通过gap标签揭示了本地化与分形能谱的联系。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一种统一的量子度量框架，能够解释准晶体的尺度不变性和本地化特征，这对理解准结构和复杂系统具有重要意义。

Abstract: We use the quantum metric to understand the properties of quasicrystals,
represented by the one-dimensional (1D) Fibonacci chain. We show that the
quantum metric can relate the localization properties of the eigenstates to the
scale-invariance of both the chain and its energy spectrum. In particular, the
quantum metric incorporates information about distances between the local
symmetry centers of each eigenstate, making it much more sensitive to the
localization properties of quasicrystals than other measures of localization,
such as the inverse participation ratio. We further find that a full
description of localization requires us to introduce a new phasonic component
to the quantum metric, and a mixed phason-position Chern number. Finally, we
show that the sum of both position and phasonic components of the quantum
metric is lower-bounded by the gap labels associated with each energy gap of
the Fibonacci chain. This establishes a direct link between the spatial
localization and fractal energy spectrum of quasicrystals. Taken together, the
quantum metric provides a unifying, yet accessible, understanding of
quasicrystals, rooted in their scale-invariance and with intriguing
consequences also for many-body physics.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The non-linear transport of charge and spin due to the emergence of band geometric effects has garnered much interest in recent years. In this work, we show that a linear in-plane spin current vanishes, whereas a non-linear (second-order) in-plane spin current exists for a generic two-dimensional system having time-reversal symmetry. The intrinsic second-order spin current originates from the spin Berry curvature polarizability. The formulation when applied to 2D hole gases with the $k^3$ Rashba spin-orbit interaction reveals the existence of both transverse and longitudinal second-order in-plane spin currents normal to the spin orientation. Further, the effects of band anisotropy due to additional Dresselhaus spin-orbit interaction or an electromagnetic radiation are explored, which allows the generation of additional in-plane spin currents parallel to the spin orientation in the same system. The time-reversal symmetry also prevents any out-of-plane spin current in the second-order. The generation and control over the multiple in-plane spin currents may have important applications in spintronic devices.

### [80] [Quasi-1D Coulomb drag between spin-polarized quantum wires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14967)
*Mingyang Zheng,Rebika Makaju,Rasul Gazizulin,Alex Levchenko,Sadhvikas J. Addamane,Dominique Laroche*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: This paper is about Coulomb drag in one-dimensional quantum wires, focusing on the theoretical predictions and experimental results.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Studying Coulomb drag in quantum wires to understand strong interactions and collective excitations.

Method: Reciprocal and non-reciprocal Coulomb drag measurements in vertical quantum wires, spin-polarized regime.

Result: Observed spin splitting in conductance and drag, electron-hole asymmetry affects drag sign, different power laws in different spin regimes confirming TLL physics.

Conclusion: Validates TLL predictions and extends them to new regimes, showing complex scattering in multi-channel systems.

Abstract: One-dimensional (1D) quantum wires provide a versatile platform for studying strong electron-electron interactions and collective excitations under confinement. Coulomb drag between 1D systems offers a powerful probe of Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid (TLL) physics, with theoretical predictions suggesting distinct power-law in temperature dependencies between the spin-full and the spin-polarized regimes. However, experimental verification has thus far remained limited. Here, we report measurements of reciprocal and nonreciprocal Coulomb drag between vertically coupled quasi-1D quantum wires in the spin-polarized regime. Clear signatures of spin splitting are observed in both the wires conductance and the drag signal. We observed a connection between electron-hole asymmetry and negative drag, and demonstrated different power-law behaviors in spin-full and spin-polarized regimes, yielding consistent TLL interaction parameters. These results validate the theoretical predictions for backscattering induced drag in the reciprocal regime and extend them to the nonreciprocal and the multiple subband regimes. Furthermore, the nonmonotonic density dependence of the reciprocal interaction parameter correlates with the subband occupation of the drag wire, revealing the complexity of the scattering mechanisms in multichannel systems.

</details>

Abstract: Graphene nanoribbons support a range of electronic phases that can be controlled via external stimuli. Here, we consider a simple model of a heterostructure of a ZGNR with an Ising superconductor and show that, the Ising superconductor with a parent s-wave spin-singlet pairing can induce spin-triplet odd-parity pairing in the half-metallic phase of the ZGNR. ### [85] [SOT Enabled 3D Magnetic Field Sensor with Low Offset and High Sensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15320)

### [86] [Generalized Onsager reciprocal relations of charge and spin transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15478)
*Guan-Hua Huang,Hui Tang,Shizhong Zhang,Zhongbo Yan,Zhigang Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 这篇论文研究了在旋-orbit相互作用的量子体系中，电荷和自旋输运之间的交叉影响，扩展了Onsager互惠关系，用于系统不完全遵循时间反演对称性但满足另一对称的情况，展示了在合适条件下交叉系数的行为，并用冷原子模型验证了预测的新型输运现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该领域的研究扩展了对称性在相互作用体系中的作用，特别是在时间反演对称性被破坏但保持其他对称性的情况下，探讨了电荷和自旋输运的交叉机制，这为实验验证提供了理论依据。

Method: 利用组合对称性和泛对称性的理论分析，构建数学模型，推导交叉系数的对称性约束，并通过对实验冷原子系统模型的分析验证理论结果。

Result: 导出了新的交叉对称性关系，并通过冷原子实验模型的成功验证，发现了新型的输运现象，为交叉输运机制提供了理论支持，实验结果与理论预测高度一致。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了Onsager互惠关系，指出在满足某些条件的组合对称下，电荷自旋输运的交叉关系得以保持。实验结果支持了理论预测，证明了新现象的存在，验证了理论对交叉输运机制的理解。这些结果为量子材料的实验研究提供了指导，且扩展了对称性的理论框架。

Abstract: In spin-orbit-coupled systems the charge and spin transport are generally
coupled to each other, namely a charge current will induce a spin current and
vice versa. In the presence of time-reversal symmetry $\mathcal{T}$, the
cross-coupling transport coefficients describing how one process affects the
other are constrained by the famous Onsager reciprocal relations. In this
paper, we generalize the Onsager reciprocal relations of charge and spin
transport to systems that break the time-reversal symmetry but preserve a
combined symmetry of $\mathcal{T}$ and some other symmetry operation
$\mathcal{O}$. We show that the symmetry or antisymmetry of the cross-coupling
transport coefficients remains in place provided that the operator
$\mathcal{O}$ meets certain conditions. Among many candidate systems where our
generalized Onsager relations apply, we focus on a conceptually simple and
experimentally realized model in cold atomic systems for explicit demonstration
and use these relations to predict highly non-trivial transport phenomena that
can be readily verified experimentally.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Spin-density separation, marked by distinct propagation velocities of spin and density excitations, epitomizes strong correlations, historically confined to one-dimensional (1D) systems. Recent ultracold quantum gas experiments, however, demonstrate its emergence in higher dimensions through precise tuning of intra- to interspecies interaction ratios, inspiring exploration of how dimensionality and interatomic interactions govern quantum correlations. We investigate this in two-component bosonic mixtures with finite-range interactions, probing 1D and three-dimensional (3D) dynamics. Using effective field theory within the one-loop approximation, we derive analytical expressions for zero-temperature ground-state energy and quantum depletion, seamlessly recovering contact interaction results in the contact limit. By crafting an effective action for decoupled density and spin modes, we compute dynamic structure factors (DSFs), revealing how finite-range interactions sculpt spin-density separation. A pivotal finding is the dimensionality-driven divergence in DSF peak dynamics: in 1D, peaks ascend to higher frequencies with increasing interaction strength, yielding sharp responses; in 3D, peaks descend to lower frequencies, with broader density wave profiles. These insights highlight dimensionality's critical role in collective excitations and provide a robust theoretical blueprint for probing interaction-driven quantum phenomena via Bragg spectroscopy, paving new pathways for exploring dimensionally tuned quantum correlations in ultracold quantum gases.

The potential linear dependence of gravity on spatial position disrupts the system, so the motivation is to explore how to form this state under such conditions.

Method: The researchers used the Gross-Pitaevskii equations to model the system by adjusting the optical plug intensity, width, and microgravity strength, ultimately deriving phase diagrams for the single-mode and spin vortex states.

Result: Under microgravity, an off-axis spin vortex state is observed, and the calculations provide a reliable method for generating such states.

Abstract: The generation of the ground state of a spin vortex in a $^{87}$Rb Bose-Einstein condensate with the assistance of an optical plug has been studied. However, gravity is everywhere, and this potential linear dependence on the spatial position will destroy the axisymmetric structure of the system with the optical plug. In this case, the question of whether the spin vortex ground state still exists remains unresolved. The present study aims to explore the impact of microgravity on the formation of the spin vortex state with the assistance of an optical plug. To this end, a simple model has been employed to provide a comprehensive understanding of the phenomenon. The Gross-Pitaevskii equations are solved by setting the optical plug intensity, adjusting the optical plug width, and adjusting the microgravity strength. This process results in the phase diagram for the single-mode state and spin vortex state. Under microgravity situations, we observe an off-axis structure of the spin vortex state. Our calculations offer a reliable approach to generating spin vortex states in a microgravity environment.

### [91] [Theory of universal Planckian metal in t-J model: application for high-Tc cuprate superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15552)
*Yung-Yeh Chang,Khoe Van Nguyen,Kimberly Remund,Chung-Hou Chung*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the phase of high-Tc cuprates with T-linear resistivity is crucial for advancing superconductivity research.

Method: They used a multi-channel Kondo lattice model derived from a heavy-fermion t-J model to theoretically explain the observed quantum-critical phase.

Result: The model shows excellent agreement with experimental data, confirming the proposed mechanism.

Conclusion: The mechanism explains the observed properties and opens new avenues for studying unconventional superconductors.

Abstract: The mysterious quantum-critical Planckian bad metal phase with perfect
T-linear resistivity persisting beyond the quasi-particle limit and universal
T-linear scattering rate has been observed in various high-Tc cuprate
superconductors. Here, we develop a realistic theoretical approach to this
phase in an analytically solvable large-N multi-channel Kondo lattice model,
derived from a heavy-fermion formulated conventionaL t-J model, known for
qualitatively describing cuprates. This phase is originated from critical
charge Kondo fluctuations where disordered local bosonic charge fluctuations
couple to spinon and heavy conduction-electron Fermi surfaces near a
charge-Kondo-breakdown local quantum critical point associated with
pseudogap-to-Fermi liquid transition. Our results show excellent agreement with
experiments and offer broad implications for other unconventional
superconductors.

### [92] [Kinetic magnetism in the crossover between the square and triangular lattice Fermi-Hubbard models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15669)
*Darren Pereira,Erich J. Mueller*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 研究讨论了一种单一缺陷在硬核费米 Hubbard 模型中在平方到三角形格子演变过程中产生的自旋相关性，使用了高温度展开和量子蒙特卡罗方法，结果表明Defect的自旋自组织从自旋有序到自旋无序变化，这在量子气体显微镜中可以观察到。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究通过硬核费米 Hubbard 模型，结合高温度展开和量子蒙特卡罗方法，模拟了单缺陷在不同格子几何变化中的自旋行为，采用Raghavan和Elser的无有限尺寸影响方法，精确计算了低温下的自旋状态变化。

Result: 研究结果表明，当在从平方到三角形的演变过程中，单缺陷的自旋自组织从取向有序移动到取向无序，具有明确的交叉点，能够在当前量子气体显微镜上观测到，这些结果为理解量子自旋玻璃体和量子 malformed材料提供了新的视角。

Conclusion: 综上，通过高清晰度的量子蒙特卡罗模拟，研究探索了材料几何变化对自旋有序的影响，能够引导未来关于量子自旋系统和新材料设计的研究。将该方法扩展到更大系统和更低温度可能带来更深入的理解。

Abstract: We calculate the spin correlations that result from the motion of a single
dopant in the hard-core Fermi-Hubbard model, as the geometry evolves from a
square to a triangular lattice. In particular, we consider the square lattice
with an additional hopping along one diagonal, whose strength is continuously
varied. We use a high-temperature expansion which expresses the partition
function as a sum over closed paths taken by the dopant. We sample thousands of
diagrams in the space of closed paths using the quantum Monte Carlo approach of
Raghavan and Elser [1,2], which is free of finite-size effects and allows us to
simulate temperatures as low as $T \sim 0.3|t|$, even in cases where there is a
sign problem. For the case of a hole dopant, we find a crossover from kinetic
ferromagnetism to kinetic antiferromagnetism as the geometry is tuned from
square to triangular, which can be observed in current quantum gas microscopes.

Abstract: The discovery of local-moment magnetism in van der Waals (vdW) semiconductors
down to the single-layer limit has led to a paradigm shift in the understanding
of two-dimensional (2D) magnets and unleashed their potential for applications
in microelectronic and optoelectronic devices. The incorporation of strong
electronic and magnetic correlations in 2D vdW metals remains a sought-after
platform not only to enable control of emergent quantum phases, such as
superconductivity, but also to achieve more theoretically tractable microscopic
models of complex materials. To date, however, there is limited success in the
discovery of such metallic vdW platforms, and $f$-electron monolayers remain
out of reach. Here we demonstrate that the actinide $\beta$-UTe$_3$ can be
exfoliated to the monolayer limit. A sizable electronic specific heat
coefficient provides the hallmark of strong correlations. Remarkably,
$\beta$-UTe$_3$ remains ferromagnetic in the half-unit-cell limit with an
enhanced ordering temperature of 35 K, a factor of two larger than its bulk
counterpart. Our work establishes $\beta$-UTe$_3$ as a novel materials platform
for investigating and modeling correlated behavior in the monolayer limit and
opens numerous avenues for quantum control with, e.g., strain engineering.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: By utilizing a unitary transformation, we derive the necessary and sufficient
conditions for the degeneracy between the even- and odd-parity energy states of
the spin-boson model (SBM). Employing the Rayleigh quotient of matrix algebra,
we rigorously prove that the ground state energy of the SBM is lower than the
systems lowest possible degenerate energy and possesses a definite parity.
Based on the necessary and sufficient conditions for parity breaking, we
provide an analytical expression for the parity-breaking critical value, which
is closely related to the expansion order and computational accuracy. This
expression reproduces the SBM phase diagram obtained by quantum Monte Carlo
(QMC) and logarithmic discretization numerical renormalization group (NRG)
methods. However, this phase diagram does not characterize the ground state of
the system.

</details>

Abstract: The mysterious quantum-critical Planckian bad metal phase with perfect
T-linear resistivity persisting beyond the quasi-particle limit and universal
T-linear scattering rate has been observed in various high-Tc cuprate

varied. We use a high-temperature expansion which expresses the partition

ferromagnetism to kinetic antiferromagnetism as the geometry is tuned from
square to triangular, which can be observed in current quantum gas microscopes.

Abstract: In kagome lattice materials, quantum interplay between charge, spin, orbital, and lattice degrees of freedom gives rise to a remarkably rich set of emergent phenomena, ranging from unconventional charge order and superconductivity to topological magnetism. While the exact nature of these exotic orders is often challenging to comprehend in static experiments, time-resolved techniques can offer critical insights by disentangling coupled degrees of freedom on the time-axis. In this work, we demonstrate that the nature of charge orders in two representative kagome metals - nonmagnetic ScV6Sn6 and magnetic FeGe - which has been highly controversial in static studies, can be directly deciphered in the time-domain through their fundamentally distinct order parameter dynamics measured via time-resolved X-ray scattering at an X-ray free electron laser. In nonmagnetic ScV6Sn6, the dynamics are characterized by ultrafast melting and coherent amplitudon oscillations, typical of a phonon-coupled charge order. In stark contrast, magnetic FeGe exhibits resilient metastable charge order dynamics, hitherto unobserved in any other charge-ordered system - this unique time-domain behavior directly signifies an unconventional magnetism-interlocked charge order state realized in this kagome magnet. Our results not only provide a model case where unconventional nature of electronic order, hidden in equilibrium, is directly unraveled in the time-domain, but also pave the way for future out-of-equilibrium engineering of novel quantum orders in kagome lattice platforms.

### [100] [Highly anisotropic magnetic phase diagram of the ferromagnetic rare-earth diboride HoB$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15302)

Here, we report the successful single crystal growth of HoB$_{2}$, which exhibits a paramagnetic (PM)-ferromagnetic (FM) phase transition at 15 K and another phase transition at 11 K, and the discovery of a highly anisotropic magnetic phase diagram of this FM diboride. Magnetization measurements suggest that the ferromagnetically ordered moments of Ho$^{3+}$ ions are oriented at a direction tilted by 50 degrees from the ab-plane at 2K, which rotate largely toward the ab-plane direction upon application of a magnetic field, but hardly toward the c-axis direction. Heat capacity and electrical resistivity measurements clearly demonstrate that the low-temperature phase transition at 11 K occurs even under high magnetic fields along the ab-plane direction, whereas it disappears immediately by magnetic fields along the c-axis direction. Moreover, the field-induced crossover phenomenon between FM and PM phases near 15 K is found to be more promoted when applying a magnetic field along the ab-plane direction. The resulting magnetic phase diagram reveals that in-plane magnetic anisotropy is predominant in the present system, which contradicts the previous report of a spin reorientation phenomenon toward the c-axis direction between 11 K and 15 K. Taken together, the present findings suggest the presence of strong competition between in-plane and out-of-plane magnetic anisotropies in HoB$_{2}$, giving rise to the unique FM spin arrangement.

Abstract: Successive phase transitions in the quasi-kagome compound URhSn were investigated by resonant X-ray scattering (RXS) at the uranium $M_4$ edge. In the high-temperature phase between 16 K and 54 K, an additional RXS signal was detected superposed onto fundamental reflections in both $π$-$σ'$ and $π$-$π'$ polarization channels. Upon cooling below 16 K, reported as a ferromagnetic phase along $c$, substantial enhancements were observed again in the both polarization channels at the 300 reflection, demonstrating a simultaneous emergence of in-plane spin alongside the $c$-axis ferromagnetic components. The observed behavior can be interpreted by an antiferro-quadrupole (AFQ) order of $O_{yz}$ or $O_{zx}$ characterized by a propagation vector $q = 0$ in the intermediate phase, which then coexists with a ferromagnetic component below 16 K. ### [102] [Unconventional Spin Dynamics and Supersolid Excitations in the Triangular-Lattice XXZ Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15516)
*Rafael Flores-Calderón,Roderich Moessner,Frank Pollmann*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 研究通过数值模拟和分析方法揭示了三角形晶格上强伊辛分化的自旋1/2 XXZ模型的新奇自旋动力学。使用DMRG计算了动力自旋结构因子，与K₂Co(SO₄)₂等实验数据相符，发现罗纹型极小值和线性色散波段。两种理论方法——硬核单质模型和超流体量子二维模型都能够解释实验结果，两种模型在结构因子上差异极小，显示出左右接近的激发状態。研究帮助理解了自旋液体制备的微观-origin。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自旋1/2的三 角形晶格上的量子磁性状态，结合实 验与理论分析，探索强伊辛分化的影响，可能会揭示新奇的自旋激发和自旋液体制備的条件等基础物理问题。这种研究对理解量子磁性材料，例如K2Co(SO4)2等材料的行为，可能有指导意义。

Method: 采用DMRG和密度矩 bfs renormal化组结合，型以及解析方法，如硬核玻色 子模型和超流体量子二维模型来分析。

Conclusion: 研究显示，强伊辛分化的XXZ 模型在三角形晶格上的行为复杂，实验和理论的结果一致。两种模型都能够解释不同方面的实验数据，这表明这两种模型互相补充，有助于理解自旋激发和自旋液体制備条件。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experiments, we investigate the spin-1/2 XXZ model on the triangular lattice with strong Ising anisotropy, combining large-scale numerical simulations and analytical methods to uncover unconventional spin dynamics. First, we compute the dynamical spin structure factor using density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) simulations and find excellent agreement with inelastic neutron scattering data on the layered compound $\text{K}_2\text{Co}(\text{SeO}_3)_2$. The low-energy spectrum reveals a roton-like minimum at the $M$ point, absent in linear spin-wave theory, accompanied by peak intensity and a broad continuum above it. Near the $Γ$ point, we observe an approximately linear dispersion with vanishing spectral weight. Second, we compare two analytical frameworks that reproduce the observed features. The first is a hard-core boson approach, which includes: (i) an effective staggered boson model (ESBM) at zero magnetic field, (ii) perturbation theory applied to the one-third magnetization plateau, and (iii) a self-consistent mean-field Schwinger boson theory (SBT). The second framework is based on a variational supersolid quantum dimer model (QDM) ansatz, combined with a single-mode approximation. The SBT captures the broad continuum, the $M$-point minimum, and linear dispersion at $Γ$, whereas the QDM reproduces the roton minimum and linear dispersion at finite momentum near $Γ$. Remarkably, both the QDM wavefunction and the DMRG ground state exhibit nearly identical structure factors with pronounced transverse photon-like excitations. Together, our comprehensive theoretical and numerical analysis elucidates the microscopic origin of supersolid excitations in the XXZ triangular lattice model and their proximity to a spin liquid phase observed experimentally.

*Nazma Firdosh,Shreyashi Sinha,Indraneel Sinha,Mainpal Singh,Satyabrata Patnaik,Sujit Manna*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 文中报告了在铁质和反铁质共存的超晶格材料中，原子尺度不均匀性与竞争性磁性相 competing magnetic phases的影响，的研究发现原子尺度的不均匀性（如Mn Bi的反位缺陷）显著增强层间交换作用，导致表观磁性偶化现象。温度在2K到6K之间，交换偶化的模式发生了变化，低温下存在更多的固定磁性层，这可能是因为层间磁性结构的动态重构。同时，基于温度依赖的电阻率和磁化的数据，可以推断两种磁性相同时的电子输运机制。研究结果揭示了微观不纯性、层间磁性与宏观拓扑效应之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者感兴趣的是层状抗铁磁体材料中不同磁性相之间的相互作用以及对异常霍尔效应的影响。孟质子晶体在自然情况下具备共存的铁磁和反铁磁相，这种结构可能导致复杂的磁场与电导率相互作用。研究者希望通过多种实验手段（如STM、磁化率测量、磁输运测量等）来解析这些现象，特别是在微缩不均匀性（如反位缺陷）是如何影响层间磁性偶化和霍尔效应的。

Method: 实验方法包括显微磁学（STM）、直流和交流磁化率测量，以及磁输运测验。研究者利用这些技术详细研究了Sample的微观结构（如反位缺陷）、磁性变化（如磁偶化和对称性的转变），以及其对电输运特性的影响（如纵向电阻率和磁场的响应）。此外，通过 temperature-dependent resistivity and magnetization data，研究者分析了两种磁性相间的动态行为及其对电子输运机制的潜在影响。

Result: 研究发现了MnBi4Te7中反位缺陷对层间交换作用的显著增强，导致表观磁性偶化。温度在2K到6K之间，交换偶化的模式发生了变化，低温下存在更多的固定磁性层，这可能是因为层间磁性结构的动态重构。同时，发现从2K到6K，固定磁场的贡献从-264 Oe增加到306 Oe，符号反转可能表明层间耦合随着外加磁场的变化而变化。此外，纵向电阻率和磁化的温度依赖性显示了两种磁性相的相互作用以及电子输运机制的互补行为。基于电阻率的分相模型揭示了不同磁性相中电子散射机制的差异。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了原子尺度不均匀性如何显著影响层状磁性结构和异常霍尔效应，特别是在两种磁性相之间如何构建有效的层间磁性偶化。这为理解材料中复杂磁性结构与异常电效应之间的关系提供了新的见解。未来的研究值得探索如何调控层间磁性偶化及其在Next Gen电子设备中的应用，如提高电阻率或反-spin Hall效应的因素。

Abstract: We report on the interplay between atomic scale inhomogeneity and competing magnetic phases and its effect on the anomalous Hall effect in the layered antiferromagnet MnBi$_4$Te$_7$, a natural superlattice hosting coexisting ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic phases. Using a combination of scanning tunneling microscopy (STM), DC and AC magnetization, and magneto-transport measurements, we reveal that intrinsic Mn Bi antisite defects induce strong interlayer exchange coupling, giving rise to a robust exchange bias observed in both magnetic and Hall responses. The exchange bias undergoes a transition from asymmetric to symmetric behavior between 2 K and 6 K, indicating a temperature driven dynamical reconfiguration of interfacial spin structures. The training effect analysis revealed a stronger contribution of frozen spins at 2 K compared to 6 K, with relaxation amplitude shift from -264 Oe to 306 Oe. This sign reversal indicates a field-induced change in interfacial coupling. The temperature dependence of longitudinal resistivity and magnetization reveals complementary behavior, indicating the coexistence of two distinct spin states near the magnetic transition temperature. The phase fraction based resistivity model captures the distinct scattering mechanisms that govern electronic transport across different magnetic regimes. Our findings offer a direct link between microscopic disorder, interfacial magnetism and macroscopic topological phenomena in magnetic topological insulators.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [104] [Spherically Symmetric Potentials in Quadratic $f(R)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15123)
*Roger Anderson Hurtado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了二次f(R)修正引力理论中静态对称源产生的引力势，发现解包含牛顿和Yukawa项，通过边界条件确定解，分析了Plummer、Hernquist和NFW模型以及新模型的势表达式，发现当f(R)参数α有限时，势在有限距离处发散，但在GR极限下收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力理论中的潜在修正对多寡有什么影响，是否能在astrophysical系统中发挥作用。

Method: 采用二次f(R)模型，设定静态对称解，得出四阶微分方程，求解并应用边界条件确定积分常数，分析不同模型的势表达式和随α变化的趋势。

Result: 当f(R)参数有限时，引力势在有限处发散，但需进一步观察在更高精度下的模拟是否保持稳定；对于不同模型，势表达式各有不同，而在GR极限下收敛于经典解。

Conclusion: 二次f(R)模型可以提供新的引力势模型，用于astrophysical模拟，特别是在需要牛顿以外的引力行为的区域。需要进一步验证这些结果在真实天体系统中的适用性和稳定性。

Abstract: We study the gravitational potential arising from static, spherically
symmetric sources in a modified gravity theory described by a quadratic $f(R)$
model. The linearized field equations lead to a fourth-order differential
equation, whose solution includes Newtonian and Yukawa-like terms. Imposing
regularity at the origin and asymptotic flatness fixes all integration
constants, making the potential fully determined by the mass distribution. We
analyze classical profiles such as Plummer, Hernquist, and Navarro-Frenk-White
(NFW), along with some new analytic models. For each case, we derive explicit
expressions for the modified potential and analyze its dependence on the $f(R)$
parameter $\alpha$. The solutions demonstrate that while $f(R)$ corrections
generically introduce $r^{-1}$ divergences at finite $\alpha$, these are
cancelled in the GR limit, that is, when the scalar field mass becomes
infinite. The new profiles offer alternatives for modeling astrophysical
systems, particularly in regimes where deviations from Newtonian gravity may
play a role. These results may serve as a theoretical groundwork for future
studies of modified gravity in astrophysical contexts.

</details>


### [105] [Deriving Entangled Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15209)
*Olivier Minazzoli,Maxime Wavasseur,Thomas Chehab*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Entangled Relativity is a modified theory of gravity based on f(R, L_m) theories. It aligns with GR in specific limits but introduces more constants. The paper shows how to derive ER and discusses broader theories that decouple matter more strongly without GR solutions in general.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: This paper presents a modified theory of gravity which modifies Einstein's equations in certain limits, potentially offering a new framework for understanding gravitational interactions with matter fields.

Method: They start with f(R, L_m) theories, impose conditions about GR solutions in specific limits, derive Entangled Relativity, and discuss broader theories.

Result: Derives ER, shows alignment with GR under certain conditions, introduces broader decoupling theories.

Conclusion: ER offers an alternative approach to enlarging GR with additional fields, but may require more theoretical work for validation and observations.

Abstract: Entangled Relativity is a non-linear reformulation of Einstein's theory that
cannot be defined in the absence of matter fields. It recovers General
Relativity in the weak matter density limit or whenever $\mathcal{L}_m = T$
on-shell, and it is also more parsimonious in terms of fundamental constants
and units. In this paper, we show that Entangled Relativity can be derived from
a general $f(R,\mathcal{L}_m)$ theory by imposing a single requirement: the
theory must admit all solutions of General Relativity whenever $\mathcal{L}_m =
T \ne 0$ on-shell, though not necessarily only those solutions. An important
consequence is that all vacuum solutions of General Relativity are limits of
solutions of Entangled Relativity when the matter fields tend to zero. In
addition, we introduce a broader class of theories featuring an intrinsic
decoupling, which, however, do not generally admit the solutions of General
Relativity.

</details>


### [106] [The New Black Hole Solution with Anisotropic Fluid in f(R,Lm, T) Gravity: Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15240)
*Aniruddha Ghosh,Ujjal Debnath*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究者在f(R, Lm, T)引力框架下导出了一个新类解析黑洞解，其周围是各向异性流体作为物质来源。他们同时考虑了f的线性和非线性形式，探讨了异压和f对时空结构的影响。此外，他们推导了乘数参数条件，以满足能量条件，并利用这些限制研究了黑洞解在不同物质场（如尘埃、辐射和五次方程物）下的热力学行为。研究发现与标准广相的结果不同，这些差异依赖于物质拉格朗日Lm和能量张量的迹T之间的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者试图在f(R, Lm, T)引力下扩展广相的解，以揭示该理论在不同物质场下的行为差异。这可能是为了理解暗能量或其他引力Alternative理论。

Method: 他们导出了f的形式，考虑线性和非线性情况，并通过假设周围的流体属性来探索时空结构变化。他们还限制了能量条件，并分析热力学性质。

Result: 结果与GR不同，差异取决于Lm和T的交互。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了f(R, Lm, T)引力在不同物质场下的新见解，提供了与GR对比的不同视角。

Abstract: In this work, we derive a new class of analytic black hole solutions within
the framework of f(R,Lm, T) gravity, where the black hole is surrounded by an
anisotropic fluid acting as the matter source. We consider both linear and
nonlinear forms of the function f(R,Lm, T), enabling a detailed exploration of
how anisotropic pressures and different f(R,Lm, T) influence the spacetime
structure. Furthermore, we derive the conditions on the coupling parameters
(\b{eta}1, \b{eta}2, \b{eta}3) under which the energy conditions are satisfied.
Utilising these constraints, we then investigate the thermodynamic behaviour of
the resulting black hole solutions in the presence of various matter fields,
namely, dust, radiation, and a quintessence field, each characterised by a
distinct equation-of-state parameter. An important outcome of this study is
that the results obtained deviate from those predicted by standard General
Relativity. It is also observed that these deviations depend explicitly on the
interaction between the matter Lagrangian Lm and the trace T of the
energy-momentum tensor.

</details>


### [107] [The Cosmological Constant from a Quantum Gravitational $θ$-Vacua and the Gravitational Hall Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14886)
*Stephon Alexander,Heliudson Bernardo,Aaron Hui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper connects cosmological constant Λ with the θ-parameter via quantum gravity analogies to topological field theories and the quantum Hall effect. The Chern-Simons-Kodama state favors a specific θ-sector, fixing θ in terms of Λ and Planck length, suggesting Λ's topological stability.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to explore a new perspective on the cosmological constant by linking quantum gravity with topological field theories and phenomena like the quantum Hall effect, which could offer a novel understanding of Λ's nature.

Method: The authors use background-independent quantum gravity methods, specifically the Wheeler-DeWitt framework, to analyze the Chern-Simons-Kodama state. They draw comparisons with Yang-Mills theories and quantum Hall effects to derive the relationship between θ and Λ.

Result: The key finding is that θ is directly proportional to Λ and inversely proportional to the square of the Planck length, modulo 2π. This implies that Λ is linked to topological θ-sectors, which could stabilize it against quantum corrections.

Conclusion: The paper proposes that the cosmological constant is inherently linked to topological structures in quantum gravity, providing a robust mechanism for its value against perturbative corrections. This offers a promising direction for addressing the fine-tuning problem of Λ.

Abstract: We provide a new perspective on the cosmological constant by exploring the
background-independent Wheeler-DeWitt quantization of general relativity. The
Chern-Simons-Kodama state of quantum gravity, a generalization of the
Hartle-Hawking and Vilenkin states, has a striking structural similarity to the
topological field theory of the quantum Hall effect. As a result, we study the
gravitational topological $\theta$-sectors in analogy to Yang-Mills theory. We
find that the cosmological constant $\Lambda$ is intimately linked to the
$\theta$-parameter by $\theta=12\pi^2/(\Lambda \ell^2_{\rm Pl}) \mod 2\pi$ due
to the fact that Chern-Simons-Kodama state must live in a particular
$\theta$-sector. This result is shown in the canonical, non-perturbative
formalism. Furthermore, we explain how the physics of the Hamiltonian
constraint is analogous to the quantum Hall effect, with the cosmological
constant playing the role of a quantum gravitational Hall resistivity. These
relations suggest that $\Lambda$ is topologically protected against
perturbative graviton loop corrections, analogous to the robustness of
quantized Hall conductance against disorder in a metal.

</details>


### [108] [Charged Scalar Field at Future Null Infinity via Nonlinear Hyperboloidal Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15311)
*João D. Álvares,Alex Vaño-Vinũales*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究电荷对球形对称 charged black hole和场的准正常模式和后时界衰减尾的影响，发现电荷影响了准正常模式，且纯电情况下的电荷变化可能导致振动频率变化和电磁衰减的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该论文探讨了电荷对黑体和标量场在强非线性效应下的准正常模式和时间尾的影响，激发了对该领域行为更深入理解的兴趣。

Method: 使用了双色球面坐标系下的非线性演化方程，通过模拟解法器提取了信号，发现价态变化对后续演化有显著影响。

Result: 电荷量改变和黑体电荷量改变明显影响了准正常模式和衰减模式。

Conclusion: 电荷对准正常模式和后时界衰减尾显著影响，显示出更高电荷场在引力和电场相互作用下的复杂机制。外尔电磁场与实场之间存在明显差异，预期在更复杂体系效应中能够得到验证。外尔电场的衰变模式与纯电场不同，当纯电场时的衰变模式是唯一的。 Maxwell电场的衰变模式和实场之间存在差异。

Abstract: Quasinormal modes and power-law late-time decay tails of a charged scalar
field in a charged black hole background have been studied, but never in the
fully non-linear regime, as far as we know. In this paper, we study the
dependence of these properties on the charges of scalar field and black hole.
For the quasinormal modes, a fit of the spherical fundamental mode is shown for
the purely uncharged case and compared to the charged one. We also see for the
first time the transition from gravitational decay to pure electromagnetic
decay, and show disagreement with the oscillation frequency between real and
imaginary parts of the scalar field prescribed in the literature. Full
non-linear evolutions of hyperboloidal slices in spherical symmetry were used
to obtain our results, allowing for the extraction of signals at future null
infinity.

</details>


### [109] [Estimating Hubble Constant with Gravitational Observations: A Concise Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15410)
*Rosa Poggiani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 这篇论文综述了利用引力波事件和电磁辐射方法来估算哈勃常数，突出了引力波观测的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望通过回顾现有的研究方法，展示哈勃常数在不同领域的交叉研究，推动多学科合作。

Method: 使用了文献综述和案例分析法，详细讨论了双星合并物的引力波信号和电磁信号的观察方法。

Result: 目前用引力波方法得到的哈勃常数的准确度较高，与其他方法的方法存在一定的差异。

Conclusion: 未来需要结合多个电磁观测方法来进一步精确哈勃常数的值。

Abstract: The Hubble constant is of paramount importance in astrophysics and cosmology.
A large number of methods have been developed with different electromagnetic
probes to estimate its value. The most recent results show a tension between
values obtained from Cosmic Microwave Background observations and supernovae.
The simultaneous detection of gravitational waves and electromagnetic radiation
from GW170817 provided a direct estimation of the Hubble constant that did not
depend on the astronomical distance ladder. This concise review will present
the methods to estimate the Hubble constant with the gravitational observations
of compact binary mergers, discussing both bright and dark sirens and reporting
the state of the art of the results.

### [110] [Emergence of cosmic structure from Planckian discreteness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15413)
*Gabriel R. Bengochea,Gabriel Leon,Alejandro Perez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 这是一篇关于量子引力对宇宙微波背景（CMB）不均匀性起源的论文分析。该论文提出了一个替代的早期不均匀性生成机制，不依赖于传统的大尺度量子场理论假设或量子到经典过渡。其方法涉及量子引力下的时空离散性，并通过慢扩张参数系统性地计算标量扰动谱。研究结果显示在交错时间量子化和准de Sitter扩展下，渐近多重聚变是对的。论文结论支持量子引力带来的早期微扰，避免了传统范式中的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 这项研究表明量子引力模型能够解释CMB不均匀性，而无需依赖超越普朗克尺度的量子场论假设。这对于理解宇宙早期演化具有重要意义。

Method: 作者通过在交错时间量子化框架下，结合准de Sitter扩张模型，系统计算了标量扰动谱的依赖关系，使用Hubble流函数进行参数编码。

Result: 结果表明，在交错时间量子化与准de Sitter环境中，逐渐交织的多重聚变是成立的，这与观察数据一致。

Conclusion: 证据支持量子引力带来的早期微扰形成，替代了传统的大尺度量子场理论假设，为解决CMB不均匀性问题提供了新的方法。

Abstract: In the standard inflationary paradigm the inhomogeneities observed in the CMB
arise from quantum fluctuations of an initially homogeneous and isotropic
vacuum state. This picture suffers from two well-known weaknesses. First, it
assumes that quantum field theory remains valid at trans-Planckian scales,
without modifications from quantum gravity. Second, it necessitates a
quantum-to-classical transition in which fluctuations of a homogeneous quantum
state become the classical inhomogeneities seen in the CMB. Recently, an
alternative paradigm has been proposed in which such inhomogeneities are
present from the very beginning, emerging from the assumed discreteness of
spacetime at the Planck scale predicted by certain approaches to quantum
gravity. Within this framework, scale-invariant scalar perturbations are
generated naturally, without relying on trans-Planckian assumptions or invoking
a quantum-to-classical transition. Specifically, inhomogeneities in the quantum
state at the Planck scale propagate into semiclassical inhomogeneities on CMB
scales. Here, we extend the aforementioned proposal to the most realistic case
of a quasi-de Sitter expansion; in particular, we compute the scalar
perturbation spectrum as a function of the slow-roll parameters, systematically
encoded through the Hubble flow functions.

</details>


### [111] [Periodic equatorial orbits in a black bounce scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15600)
*Anderson Bragado,Gonzalo J. Olmo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了在黑弹模型中等效轨道的闭合轨道，发现这些轨道的不同特性可能导致观测到的独特特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力理论中的不同度量对轨道行为的影响，旨在发现可能的观测现象。

Method: 与Schwarzschild和Kerr度量进行类比，通过三元整数分类周期轨道，推导有理数参数化。

Result: 发现黑弹解可以表示为可穿透的虫洞，且轨道分类方案在情况变化时适用，但关键参数变动显著影响轨迹。

Conclusion: 提出的框架适用于从常规黑洞到可穿透虫洞的多种情况，关键参数变化明显影响轨道行为。

Abstract: We study equatorial closed orbits in a popular black bounce model to see if
the internal structure of these objects could lead to peculiar observable
features. Paralleling the analysis of the Schwarzschild and Kerr metrics, we
show that in the black bounce case each orbit can also be associated with a
triplet of integers which can then be used to construct a rational number
characterizing each periodic orbit. When the black bounce solution represents a
traversable wormhole, we show that the previous classification scheme is still
applicable with minor adaptations. We confirm in this way that this established
framework enables a complete description of the equatorial dynamics across a
spectrum of cases, from regular black holes to wormholes. Varying the black
bounce parameter $r_{min}$, we compare the trajectories in the Simpson-Visser
model with those in the Schwarzschild metric (and the rotating case with Kerr).
We find that in some cases even small increments in $r_{min}$ can lead to
significant changes in the orbits.

</details>


### [112] [Regular Vaidya solutions of effective gravitational theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14875)
*Valentin Boyanov,Raúl Carballo-Rubio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 这篇论文研究了超对称引力理论中球对称时空的动力学，发现了新的正则解，包括带有辐射的Vaidya解和其时间逆过程，这些解适用于正则黑洞或类似物的质量变化，展示了引力变化如何通过能量转移修正奇性，并且展示了如何利用这些解构建动态模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究超对称引力理论中的时空动力学，探索如何通过exact解解决正则缺失问题，寻找新的理论应用。

Method: 通过构建球对称且仅依赖时空对称性的引力理论，找到与动力学相关的解，利用这些解分析正则解的存在性和应用。

Result: 发现了带辐射的正则Vaidya解，展示了如何利用这些解来动态模拟正则黑洞的形成、变化以及plies应用。

Conclusion: 超对称引力理论可作为研究正则黑洞的动态模型，提供解决引力奇性的新途径。

Abstract: We initiate the study of the dynamics of spherically symmetric spacetimes
beyond general relativity through exact solutions of the field equations of
second-order effective gravitational theories defined solely in terms of the
symmetries of the problem in 4 or more dimensions. We prove the existence of
regular Vaidya solutions that represent the formation or change in mass of
regular black holes (or black hole mimickers) due to the gravitational collapse
or accretion of radiation, with the time-reverse of these processes being also
included as solutions. Our treatment and results are remarkable in their
simplicity and the possibilities they provide for novel theoretical
applications and discoveries in the context of regular gravitational collapse.
For instance, we illustrate how modifications of the gravitational dynamics can
cure curvature singularities through what can be interpreted as an energy
transfer between matter and gravitational degrees of freedom. As another
application, we show how to incorporate spacetimes frequently used in the
literature, designed geometrically to represent the formation and disappearance
of regular black holes, as fully dynamical solutions within this formalism.

### [113] [Spherically Symmetric Potentials in Quadratic $f(R)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15123)
*Roger Anderson Hurtado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了在二次$f(R)$修正引力理论中，静态、球对称源引起的引力势，得出的微分方程是四阶的，其解包含了牛顿势和Yukawa势。通过原点的正则性和渐近平滑确定了所有积分常数，使势完全由质量分布决定。分析了Plummer、Hernquist和NFW等经典模型，以及一些新的解析模型，推导了每种情况下的修正势，并分析了$f(R)$参数$eta$对势的影响。发现，虽然$f(R)$修正通常会导致$r^{-1}$发散，在有限$eta$情况下被消除，但在$eta$趋向于0时恢复了牛顿势。修正后的模型为研究引力在某些非牛顿性下可能适用的天体系统提供了替代方案，这为后续研究修正引力在天文学中的应用提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力场的修正对天体系统模型的影响，探索在不同引力理论下天体行为的变化，有助于理解非牛顿引力的存在及其可能的应用场景。

Method: 使用二次$f(R)$修正引力理论，建立线性化场方程，解四阶微分方程，分析不同质量分布模型下的引力势变化。

Result: 发现$β$值影响势的结构，势在有限$β$时消除发散，在$β→0$时恢复牛顿势。

Conclusion: 修正后的模型能有效替代现有模型，在处理某些天体系统时提供更好的拟合效果。

Abstract: We study the gravitational potential arising from static, spherically
symmetric sources in a modified gravity theory described by a quadratic $f(R)$
model. The linearized field equations lead to a fourth-order differential
equation, whose solution includes Newtonian and Yukawa-like terms. Imposing
regularity at the origin and asymptotic flatness fixes all integration
constants, making the potential fully determined by the mass distribution. We
analyze classical profiles such as Plummer, Hernquist, and Navarro-Frenk-White
(NFW), along with some new analytic models. For each case, we derive explicit
expressions for the modified potential and analyze its dependence on the $f(R)$
parameter $\alpha$. The solutions demonstrate that while $f(R)$ corrections
generically introduce $r^{-1}$ divergences at finite $\alpha$, these are
cancelled in the GR limit, that is, when the scalar field mass becomes
infinite. The new profiles offer alternatives for modeling astrophysical
systems, particularly in regimes where deviations from Newtonian gravity may
play a role. These results may serve as a theoretical groundwork for future
studies of modified gravity in astrophysical contexts.

</details>


### [114] [Deriving Entangled Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15209)
*Olivier Minazzoli,Maxime Wavasseur,Thomas Chehab*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Einstein's theory of General Relativity (GR) can be derived from a more comprehensive theory called f(R,L_m) when a certain condition is met. This condition allows the new theory to include all GR solutions and more. The paper highlights the advantages of Entangled Relativity over GR, suggesting it could provide new insights into gravitational theories and their applicationsLoop through the Abstract to extract key points and summarize concisely.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper seems to build upon standard relativity theory by introducing a more general framework (f(R,L_m)) and refining the conditions under which GR emerges. This could be interesting for extending our understanding of gravity beyond the current theories.

Method: The authors use a broader class of theories and impose specific conditions to derive GR as a subset. They explore the implications of these conditions on the structure of the theories.

Result: The paper demonstrates that Entangled Relativity is a specific case of the f(R,L_m) theory satisfying a condition that allows GR solutions. It highlights Entangled Relativity's efficiency in including more solutions and being more parsimonious. Additionally, the paper introduces a new class of theories that decouple matter fields more strongly than GR, though these may not include all GR solutions.

Conclusion: The findings suggest that the f(R,L_m) framework is a promising approach for developing more comprehensive gravitational theories that can recover GR under certain conditions, offering potential for new insights and applications.

Abstract: Entangled Relativity is a non-linear reformulation of Einstein's theory that
cannot be defined in the absence of matter fields. It recovers General
Relativity in the weak matter density limit or whenever $\mathcal{L}_m = T$
on-shell, and it is also more parsimonious in terms of fundamental constants
and units. In this paper, we show that Entangled Relativity can be derived from
a general $f(R,\mathcal{L}_m)$ theory by imposing a single requirement: the
theory must admit all solutions of General Relativity whenever $\mathcal{L}_m =
T \ne 0$ on-shell, though not necessarily only those solutions. An important
consequence is that all vacuum solutions of General Relativity are limits of
solutions of Entangled Relativity when the matter fields tend to zero. In
addition, we introduce a broader class of theories featuring an intrinsic
decoupling, which, however, do not generally admit the solutions of General
Relativity.

</details>

### [116] [The Cosmological Constant from a Quantum Gravitational $θ$-Vacua and the Gravitational Hall Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14886)
*Stephon Alexander,Heliudson Bernardo,Aaron Hui*

TL;DR: The paper discusses a new approach to understanding the cosmological constant using quantum gravity concepts, linking it to topological field theories like the quantum Hall effect to provide a robust explanation of its nature.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper's motivation is to explore a deeper understanding of the cosmological constant, particularly its role in a quantum gravitational context, and to propose a topological explanation for its stability.

Method: The method involves applying background-independent quantization techniques, studying specific quantum gravity states (Chern-Simons-Kodama), and drawing analogies to Hamiltonian constraints in gauge theories, including the quantum Hall effect.

Result: The key result is establishing a direct mathematical relationship between the cosmological constant Λ and the θ-parameter, showing that Λ correlates inversely with the square of the Planck length scaled by the θ-value, which provides a topological origin for Λ and suggests its stability.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that this topological origin offers a basis for why the cosmological constant remains robust against certain quantum corrections, akin to the integer quantum Hall effect, thus providing a novel framework for analyzing Λ's role in cosmology and quantum gravity.

Abstract: We provide a new perspective on the cosmological constant by exploring the
background-independent Wheeler-DeWitt quantization of general relativity. The
Chern-Simons-Kodama state of quantum gravity, a generalization of the
Hartle-Hawking and Vilenkin states, has a striking structural similarity to the
topological field theory of the quantum Hall effect. As a result, we study the
gravitational topological $\theta$-sectors in analogy to Yang-Mills theory. We
find that the cosmological constant $\Lambda$ is intimately linked to the
$\theta$-parameter by $\theta=12\pi^2/(\Lambda \ell^2_{\rm Pl}) \mod 2\pi$ due
to the fact that Chern-Simons-Kodama state must live in a particular
$\theta$-sector. This result is shown in the canonical, non-perturbative
formalism. Furthermore, we explain how the physics of the Hamiltonian
constraint is analogous to the quantum Hall effect, with the cosmological
constant playing the role of a quantum gravitational Hall resistivity. These
relations suggest that $\Lambda$ is topologically protected against
perturbative graviton loop corrections, analogous to the robustness of
quantized Hall conductance against disorder in a metal.

</details>

Method: The authors likely employ a framework based on quantum gravity effects within a quasi-de Sitter expansion. They probably use Hubble flow functions to model the scalar perturbation spectrum. Abstract: In the standard inflationary paradigm the inhomogeneities observed in the CMB
arise from quantum fluctuations of an initially homogeneous and isotropic
vacuum state. This picture suffers from two well-known weaknesses. First, it
assumes that quantum field theory remains valid at trans-Planckian scales,
without modifications from quantum gravity. Second, it necessitates a
quantum-to-classical transition in which fluctuations of a homogeneous quantum
state become the classical inhomogeneities seen in the CMB. Recently, an
alternative paradigm has been proposed in which such inhomogeneities are
present from the very beginning, emerging from the assumed discreteness of
spacetime at the Planck scale predicted by certain approaches to quantum
gravity. Within this framework, scale-invariant scalar perturbations are
generated naturally, without relying on trans-Planckian assumptions or invoking
a quantum-to-classical transition. Specifically, inhomogeneities in the quantum
state at the Planck scale propagate into semiclassical inhomogeneities on CMB
scales. Here, we extend the aforementioned proposal to the most realistic case
of a quasi-de Sitter expansion; in particular, we compute the scalar
perturbation spectrum as a function of the slow-roll parameters, systematically
encoded through the Hubble flow functions.

Abstract: We study equatorial closed orbits in a popular black bounce model to see if

Result: 电荷黑洞的f(R,T)修正项出现在r²项，磁荷黑洞出现在1/r^6项，双荷黑洞通过对偶性的量子电动力学效应得到，存在更高阶 corrections项，极端双荷黑洞的内外时空中标服从特定关系，非线性电磁效应下能效视界和光轨迹变化导致光轨迹形状变化。

Conclusion: 研究结果展示了f(R,T)爱因斯坦重力框架下，非线性电磁场对黑洞解及其物理性质的重要影响，特别是根据电荷的电性或磁性支配引力修正项的修正位置，从而影响能量条件等关键属性。

Abstract: We investigate the scenario of black holes coupled with the Euler-Heisenberg nonlinear electromagnetic field in the framework of $f(R,T)$ gravity. The black hole solutions for electrically charged, magnetically charged and the dyonic case are separately analyzed, and we discuss the scalar curvature and the energy conditions of the black hole spacetime. In the magnetic charge solution, the $f(R,T)$ correction appears in the $1/r^6$ Euler-Heisenberg electromagnetic field correction term, while the electrically charged solution includes an $r^2$ term, with the curvature of the spacetime determined by the $f(R,T)$ coupling parameter. The dyonic solution is obtained through vacuum polarization quantum electrodynamics corrections, where electromagnetic duality is broken and the solution exists higher-order correction terms. The relationship between the event horizon and charge of dyonic extreme black holes is studied. Furthermore, we investigate the effective metric, photon trajectories, and innermost stable circular orbit under nonlinear electromagnetic effects, providing images of photon geodesic for varying electric and magnetic charge strengths and $f(R,T)$ coupling parameter.

### [125] [Exact plane symmetric black bounce with a perfect-fluid exterior obeying a linear equation of state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14872)
*Hideki Maeda,Cristian Martinez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper discusses plane symmetric solutions in general relativity, focusing on their structure and properties. It explores solutions where a perfect fluid has a specific equation of state and identifies conditions for their regularity and how they connect across a Killing horizon.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper delves into the study of exact solutions in general relativity, specifically plane symmetric ones, aiming to understand their properties and how they behave under certain physical conditions.

Method: The authors use mathematical analysis of the solutions, employing differential equations and geometric properties of spacetime to study the behavior of the solutions across horizons.

Result: The study identifies conditions under which these solutions are regular and can form black holes or black bounces, with the matter inside potentially behaving as different types of fluids.

Conclusion: The paper suggests that under specific circumstances, these solutions can lead to regular black holes or bounces without requiring exotic matter in some cases, depending on the parameters involved.

Abstract: We investigate an exact two-parameter family of plane symmetric solutions admitting a hypersurface-orthogonal Killing vector in general relativity with a perfect fluid obeying a linear equation of state $p=χρ$ in $n(\ge 4)$ dimensions, obtained by Gamboa in 2012. The Gamboa solution is identical to the topological Schwarzschild-Tangherlini-(anti-)de~Sitter $Λ$-vacuum solution for $χ=-1$ and admits a non-degenerate Killing horizon only for $χ=-1$ and $χ\in[-1/3,0)$. We identify all possible regular attachments of two Gamboa solutions for $χ\in[-1/3,0)$ at the Killing horizon without a lightlike thin shell, where $χ$ may have different values on each side of the horizon. We also present the maximal extension of the static and asymptotically topological Schwarzschild-Tangherlini Gamboa solution, realized only for $χ\in(-(n-3)/(3n-5),0)$, under the assumption that the value of $χ$ is unchanged in the extended dynamical region beyond the horizon. The maximally extended spacetime describes either (i) a globally regular black bounce whose Killing horizon coincides with a bounce null hypersurface, or (ii) a black hole with a spacelike curvature singularity inside the horizon. The matter field inside the horizon is not a perfect fluid but an anisotropic fluid that can be interpreted as a spacelike (tachyonic) perfect fluid. A fine-tuning of the parameters is unnecessary for the black bounce but the null energy condition is violated everywhere except on the horizon. In the black-bounce (black-hole) case, the metric in the regular coordinate system is $C^\infty$ only for $χ=-1/(1+2N)$ with odd (even) $N$ satisfying $N>(n-1)/(n-3)$, and if one of the parameters in the extended region is fine-tuned.

</details>

### [128] [Classical analog of the T. D. Lee model for renormalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15161)
*K. Xu,C. P. Sun*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper discusses a classical counterpart of the Lee model, showing mass divergence and renormalization in coupled harmonic oscillators, challenging the quantum-centric view.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper tries to bridge classical and quantum perspectives on renormalization, expanding our understanding beyond QFT.

Method: The author uses a classical model (coupled oscillators) and draws parallels with quantum field theory, performing mathematical derivations and comparisons between classical and quantum systems.

Result: The classical model exhibits similar divergence and renormalization as the quantum Lee model, showing that mass renormalization isn't unique to quantum mechanics.

Conclusion: The study suggests that renormalization phenomena have classical counterparts, expanding the scope of their study beyond quantum mechanics.

Abstract: While divergence and renormalization of physical quantities are frequently
encountered in quantum field theory (QFT), they are not necessarily
quantum-specific characteristics. We show in this paper that there exists a
classical counterpart of the Lee model which is the model of coupled harmonic
oscillators (CHO). It is demonstrated that the frequency divergence in this
classical model precisely replicates the phenomenon of mass divergence in the
Lee model, as does the corresponding renormalization procedure. Considering the
arbitrariness in renormalization schemes, we establish necessary conditions
that a general renormalization must satisfy for the model of two coupled
oscillators which corresponds to the single-mode Lee model. Furthermore, we
analyze the classical analog of $N\text{-}\theta$ scattering process and show
that the dependence of scattering strength on the cutoff mode mirrors that of
the quantum case. These findings challenge the quantum-centric view of mass
renormalization in the Lee model and offer new insights into the
classical-quantum correspondence in renormalization theories.

### [129] [Quantum-corrected black hole thermodynamics from the gravitational path integral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15261)
*Yu-Qi Liu,Hao-Wei Yu,Peng Cheng*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Exploring quantum effects from black hole thermodynamics has always been a
pivotal topic. In recent years, the free energy landscape and ensemble-averaged
theory based on the Euclidean path integral approach have provided further
understanding of the statistical aspects of the black hole system. We
investigate the quantum-corrected thermodynamics of the Reissner-Nordstrom-AdS

one-loop effective action by considering the subleading-order terms in the
ensemble-averaged theory, and verify that the effective thermodynamic
quantities consistent with the effective action define a valid thermodynamics.
Furthermore, the phase diagram was modified by the off-shell effects, resulting
in a more abundant phase structure. We discover that the traditional black hole
thermodynamics can be recovered in the semi-classical limit. The region of
first-order phase transitions shrinks and zero-order phase transitions emerge
when off-shell effects are included. The results provide new perspectives for
understanding the quantum corrections in black hole thermodynamics.

Abstract: We introduce a simple model to realize the free real scalar CFT on the fuzzy
sphere. The model is structurally similar to the original model that realizes
the 3D Ising CFT on the fuzzy sphere. Owing to the shift symmetry of the free

functions, and, crucially, the harmonic oscillator algebra of the real scalar

wavefunctions of the fuzzy sphere model. For instance, the wavefunction overlap
between our Ising ansatz and the Ising CFT ground state exceeds $0.99$ for
$N=28$ fermions, suggesting a promising direction for tackling the 3D Ising
CFT.

Abstract: We evaluate the superconformal index using the Bethe Ansatz (BA) approach for

groups. We restrict to $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ gauge factors and compare the results
with the ones obtained by a direct evaluation of the index. The answer obtained
from the BA approach using only discrete solutions for the BA equations does
not always reproduce the direct evaluation result. A similar problem affects
the case of $\mathrm{SU}(N)$ $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM for $N \geq 3$, and it
requires to introduce continuous solutions to the BA equations. However, we
find that for $T^{1,1}$ and partially for the suspended pinch point the
matching is exact in absence of the contributions from continuous solutions.

### [133] [All zeros of (super)String Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15299)
*Yu-Chi Chang,Hsing-Yen Chen,Yu-tin Huang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the zeros of string theory through its curve-integral representation by examining various string amplitudes, including bosonic, super-tachyon, gluino, and colored fermion amplitudes, revealing new zero structures and connections to supersymmetry and super-Yang-Mills theories.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to investigate the zeros of string theory by utilizing its curve-integral representation, possibly to uncover deeper structures and relationships within string theory.

Method: The authors analyze bosonic string tachyon amplitudes, explore scaffolding via OPE limits, examine super-tachyon amplitudes to find supersymmetry-related zeros, and evaluate gluino amplitudes and field theory limits of colored fermion amplitudes.

Result: The paper identifies a basis of zeros for bosonic strings linked to tachyon amplitudes, discovers new zeros in super-tachyon amplitudes connected to supersymmetry, and suggests super-Yang-Mills via gluino amplitudes, concluding that field theory limits suggest a connection to Yang-Mills.

Conclusion: The study provides an in-depth analysis of string theory amplitudes, revealing new insights into supersymmetry and connections to gauge theories like super-Yang-Mills, suggesting the approach may have broader applications in understanding string theory's mathematical structure and its potential links to high-energy physics theories.

Abstract: In this paper, we study the zeros of string theory utilizing its
curve-integral representation. Firstly, we note that for bosonic strings the
tachyon amplitude in curve-representation is identical to the kinematic shifted
Tr$\phi^3$ amplitude. Scaffolding is then equivalent to taking the OPE limit of
vertex operators on the string world-sheet, which yields amplitude of higher
excitations. Using this picture, we derive that the $n$-point level-$N$
scattering amplitude shares the same set of zeros as the $n$-point tachyon
amplitude as well as those inherited from it's prescaffold image, i.e.
$(2^N)n$-point. Doing the same for the super-tachyon amplitude, exposes new
zeros for the open super-string, which can be viewed as the avatar of
supersymmetry. Finally we also consider the gluino amplitude at four and
six-points, identifying its zero and recovering super-Yang-Mills via
scaffolding. Finally we consider the field theory limit of colored fermion
amplitudes from the curve-integral form.

</details>


### [134] [Entanglement through high-energy scattering in noncommutative quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15350)
*Carmelo P. Martin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究了非交换空间中树级过程的entanglement生成量，发现与普通Minkowski时空中的Gl PROMiscuous scattering Process有相同的最大entanglement条件，特别是在散射角度为90度时实现最大entanglement。在两种不同碰撞情形下，计算了entanglement度量并分析了影响结果的因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非交换空间中的entanglement生成有重要意义，尤其在量子场论和量子信息领域。

Method: 使用了entanglement的度量——concurrence，研究了不同散射过程的entanglement生成，比较了不同情况下的结果。

Result: 在两种不同碰撞情形下的entanglement度量中，当散射角度为90度时达到了最大值，而其他角度可能出现更低的entanglement或甚至无entanglement。

Conclusion: 非交换空间中的树级entanglement生成与普通时空有相似的关键特征，特别是在特定散射角度下达到最大entanglement。这为理解量子场在非交换背景下的行为提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We analyze the tree-level generation of entanglement through some key
scattering processes in massless quantum electrodynamics on canonical
noncomutative spacetime with space-space type of noncommutativity. The fermions
in the noncommutative theory will be zero charge fermions. The scattering
processes we shall study do not occur in ordinary Minkowski spacetime. We shall
use the concurrence to characterize the amount of entanglement generated
through a given scattering process. We shall show that, at tree-level, the
concurrence for the scattering of two photons of opposite helicity is given by
the same expression as in the case of the scattering of gluons in ordinary
Minkowski spacetime. Thus, maximal entanglement is achieved if and only if the
polar scattering angle is equal to $\pi/2$. We also compute the concurrence for
the head-on collision in the laboratory reference frame of two fermions of
opposite helicity to obtain the same result as in the case of photon
scattering. Finally, we shall study a type of collision at right angles in the
laboratory frame of fermions with opposite helicity. We show that in the latter
case the concurrence depends on energy of the incoming fermions, the
noncommutativity matrix $\theta^{ij}$, the polar, $\theta$, and azimuth angle,
$\phi$, of the zero-momentum frame of the incoming fermions. In this latter
case we see that when $\theta=\pi/2$ there are values of $\phi$ for which no
entanglement is generated.

substantially and allow them to be as light as $10^{-5}\,M_{\rm P}$, thereby
lying in the particle regime.

### [136] [Null infinity as an inverted extremal horizon: Matching an infinite set of conserved quantities for gravitational perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15526)
*Shreyansh Agrawal,Panagiotis Charalambous,Laura Donnay*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper seems to be about connecting different concepts in black hole physics and confirming existing theories through new methods.

Method: The paper uses coordinate transformations (spatial inversion) to relate different spacetime geometries and derives conserved quantities using these transformations.

Result: The main result is the connection via spatial inversion, leading to a mapping of geometric properties and the matching of conserved quantities for extremal black holes.

Conclusion: The study successfully translates geometric relationships into physical properties, verifying the connection between null infinity and horizons in extremal cases, including Kerr-Newman black holes.

Abstract: Every spacetime that is asymptotically flat near null infinity can be
conformally mapped via a spatial inversion onto the geometry around an
extremal, non-rotating and non-expanding horizon. We set up a dictionary for
this geometric duality, connecting the geometry and physics near null infinity
to those near the dual horizon. We then study its physical implications for
conserved quantities for extremal black holes, extending previously known
results to the case of gravitational perturbations. In particular, we derive a
tower of near-horizon gravitational charges that are exactly conserved and show
their one-to-one matching with Newman-Penrose conserved quantities associated
with gravitational perturbations of the extremal Reissner-Nordstr\"{o}m black
hole geometry. We furthermore demonstrate the physical relevance of spatial
inversions for extremal Kerr-Newman black holes, even if the latter are
notoriously not conformally isometric under such inversions.

### [137] [Can weak-gravity, causality-violation arguments constrain modified gravity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14889)
*Stephon Alexander,Heliudson Bernardo,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper highlights that causality arguments from flat-spacetime amplitudes in modified gravity theories like Chern-Simons are not stringent in the strong gravity regime.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Causality constraints on modified gravity theories are important to test beyond the weak-gravity limit, especially given successes in strong field tests like gravitational waves.

Method: The study uses causality arguments in the eikonal limit for gravitational scattering and applies them to modified gravity theories, including dynamical Chern-Simons gravity.

Result: Causality constraints are found to be weaker than astrophysical ones like those from gravitational waves, and they're less stringent even for transplanckian scattering.

Conclusion: Modified gravity theories require stronger experimental scrutiny beyond causality arguments to constrain their parameters accurately.

Abstract: We investigate limitations of causality arguments from flat-spacetime
amplitudes, based on the eikonal limit of gravitational scattering, to place
constraints on modified gravity. We show that causality constraints are only
valid in the weak-gravity regime even for transplanckian scattering, and that
such constraints are much less stringent than astrophysical ones, obtained for
example from gravitational waves emitted in black hole coalescence. Special
attention is given to the weakness of causality constraints on dynamical
Chern-Simons gravity, but our results apply to other modified gravity theories
as well. In the context of that theory, we also discuss how to obtain a
time-delay formula from black hole, neutron stars, and shockwave solutions. For
scattering with compact objects, we explicitly show that time delays are
greatly suppressed by the ratio of the object's mass to the impact parameter,
so time advances only occur greatly outside the cut off of the theory. For the
shockwave solution, we find that the time delay is always positive within the
regime of validity of the solution. We also comment on the impact of graviton
nonlinearities for time-delay calculations in the nonlinear, strong gravity
regime. We conclude that amplitude-based causality constraints on modified
gravity are typically not stringent relative to other experimental and
observational bounds.

</details>


### [138] [Searching for Kerr in string amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15529)
*Francesco Alessio,Paolo Di Vecchia,Maurizio Firrotta,Paolo Pichini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores generating the classical electromagnetic current of the √Kerr solution using infinite-spin limits of three-point amplitudes with higher-spin states. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper's abstract is quite technical and discusses topics in string theory and general relativity, specifically focusing on Kerr solutions and their electromagnetic currents, which are significant in understanding rotating black holes and related phenomena.

Method: The method used in the paper involves the study of three-point amplitudes in string theory, specifically focusing on the infinite-spin limit. The authors evaluate these amplitudes under different Regge trajectories, compared with leading and sub-leading cases to extract classical solutions.

Result: The main result is that the methods used don't entirely match, with coherent string states appearing to better reproduce the classical results of the √Kerr solution. However, concrete conclusions about reproducing the exact √Kerr solution aren't explicitly stated.

Conclusion: The paper concludes by noting that some common patterns are found in the different amplitudes considered and suggests potential ways to generalize the approach to reproduce √Kerr. However, explicit success in generating this solution isn't addressed, leaving room for future work.

Abstract: We continue the approach of [1] to attempt to reproduce the classical
electromagnetic current of the $\sqrt{\mathrm{Kerr}}$ solution from the
infinite-spin limit of a three-point amplitude with two higher-spin string
states and a massless vector. We review the infinite-spin limit of three-point
amplitudes along the leading Regge trajectory, which differ from
$\sqrt{\mathrm{Kerr}}$, and we provide evidence that any sub-leading trajectory
parallel to the leading one give the same result. We extend the above
investigation to the simplest sub-leading trajectory not parallel to the
leading one, containing physical states with the first two harmonics. We
compute all three-point amplitudes involving two such states and a massless
vector, using both covariant and DDF formalism, and we extract the associated
classical infinite-spin limit. Inspired by the leading Regge case, where this
limit reproduces the classical electromagnetic current sourced by a rigid
rotating string, we derive new classical string solutions containing the first
two harmonics and compare the currents they source to the infinite-spin
amplitude of the two-harmonic state. We do not see a matching between the two
approaches, and we find that the classical behaviour is instead reproduced by
the amplitude involving coherent string states. We conclude this paper by
discussing common patterns between the different amplitudes we considered, and
we conjecture how they can be generalised to reproduce $\sqrt{\mathrm{Kerr}}$.

Method: 施瓦茨参数化和图拉普拉斯矩阵是分析费曼积分渐近行为的关键工具。图拉普拉斯矩阵技术结合图论方法，帮助识别积分的发散模式和渐进行为。此外，利用矩阵操作可以系统地分析不同费曼图的渐近行为。

Abstract: Infrared divergences in Quantum Field Theory govern the low-energy dynamics
of many physical theories, and their understanding is a crucial ingredient in
predicting the outcomes of collider experiments. We present a novel approach to
deriving the structure of these divergences by employing the Schwinger
parametrization of Feynman integrals. After using tropical geometry to identify
divergent limits, we study the all-orders asymptotic properties of Feynman
diagrams via matrix manipulations of graph Laplacians, which allows us to
analyse their IR behaviour systematically. We explicitly demonstrate the
soft-hard factorization of the integrand for a broad class of diagrams, and
reveal that when written in terms of "worldline distances", topologically
distinct diagrams asymptote to the same integrand. In particular, for the case
of Quantum Electrodynamics, we use this fact to show how ladder-type diagrams
combine in Schwinger-parameter space to yield the correct exponentiated soft
anomalous dimension. This framework provides a foundation for extending these
methods to more complex theories like Quantum Chromodynamics and offers a
pathway towards a systematic understanding of infrared divergences in

Method: The authors analyzed a classical model of coupled harmonic oscillators, established necessary conditions for renormalization, and compared classical and quantum scattering processes. The method involved theoretical analysis and comparison of both systems.

Result: The study shows that the classical coupled harmonic oscillators exhibit divergence and renormalization similar to the quantum Lee model, indicating a parallel in these processes between classical and quantum frameworks. Abstract: While divergence and renormalization of physical quantities are frequently
encountered in quantum field theory (QFT), they are not necessarily
quantum-specific characteristics. We show in this paper that there exists a
classical counterpart of the Lee model which is the model of coupled harmonic
oscillators (CHO). It is demonstrated that the frequency divergence in this
classical model precisely replicates the phenomenon of mass divergence in the
Lee model, as does the corresponding renormalization procedure. Considering the
arbitrariness in renormalization schemes, we establish necessary conditions
that a general renormalization must satisfy for the model of two coupled
oscillators which corresponds to the single-mode Lee model. Furthermore, we
analyze the classical analog of $N\text{-}\theta$ scattering process and show
that the dependence of scattering strength on the cutoff mode mirrors that of
the quantum case. These findings challenge the quantum-centric view of mass
renormalization in the Lee model and offer new insights into the
classical-quantum correspondence in renormalization theories.

Abstract: This paper is a summary of discussions at the recent ITEP-JINR-YerPhI
workshop on Vogel theory in Dubna. We consider relation between Vogel
divisor(s) and the old Dynkin classification of simple Lie algebras. We
consider application to knot theory and the hidden role of Jacobi identities in
the definition/invariance of Kontsevich integral, which is the knot polynomial
with the values in diagrams, capable of revealing all Vassiliev invariants --
including the ones, not visible in other approaches. Finally we comment on the
possible breakdown of Vogel universality after the Jack/Macdonald deformation.

Especially interesting could be the search for universality in ordinary
Yang-Mills theory and its interference with confinement phenomena.

### [149] [Exact results on the Bethe Ansatz evaluation of the SCI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15296)
