<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The exploration of the superconformal index is a significant tool in understanding the dynamics and properties of supersymmetric gauge theories. Evaluating this index accurately can provide insights into the dualities and structures inherent in these theories, particularly in the context of quiver gauge theories which are known for their rich vacuum structures and dualities.

Method: The authors employ the Bethe Ansatz (BA) approach to evaluate the superconformal index for the specified gauge theories. They restrict their analysis to systems with a small number of gauge groups, particularly focusing on SU(2) configurations. The method involves solving the BA equations and comparing the obtained results with direct evaluations of the index to assess discrepancies.

Result: The study reveals that the BA approach yields results that are inconsistent with direct evaluations in certain cases, primarily when dealing with SU(N) gauge groups for N≥3. However, in specific instances such as the T^{1,1} geometry and parts of the suspended pinch point, the BA method accurately reproduces the index without requiring the inclusion of continuous solutions to the BA equations.

Conclusion: The findings suggest that while the Bethe Ansatz approach is a powerful tool for evaluating the superconformal index, its application must take into account the presence of both discrete and continuous solutions to the BA equations. This nuanced approach leads to more accurate and reliable evaluations of the superconformal index across different gauge theory configurations.

Abstract: We evaluate the superconformal index using the Bethe Ansatz (BA) approach for
4d $\mathcal{N}=1$ toric quiver gauge theories with a small amount of gauge
groups. We restrict to $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ gauge factors and compare the results
with the ones obtained by a direct evaluation of the index. The answer obtained
from the BA approach using only discrete solutions for the BA equations does
not always reproduce the direct evaluation result. A similar problem affects
the case of $\mathrm{SU}(N)$ $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM for $N \geq 3$, and it
requires to introduce continuous solutions to the BA equations. However, we
find that for $T^{1,1}$ and partially for the suspended pinch point the
matching is exact in absence of the contributions from continuous solutions.

### [150] [All zeros of (super)String Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15299)
*Yu-Chi Chang,Hsing-Yen Chen,Yu-tin Huang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the zeros of string theory using a curve-integral approach. It studies bosonic and super-tachyon amplitudes, finds new zeros in the supercase, and discusses field theory limits with fermions, suggesting rich implications for string dynamics and field theory models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper delves into the complex interplay between string theory and particle physics by examining scattering amplitudes, aiming to uncover new mathematical properties and physical insights related to the underlying theories.

Method: The authors utilize a curve-integral representation, focusing on vertex operator OPE limits and leveraging supersymmetry to derive scattering amplitudes. They analyze both bosonic and super-tachyons, exploring zeros and their implications, while also considering field theory limits with fermions.

Result: Through detailed calculations, the paper identifies new zeros in super-tachyon amplitudes and connects field theory models to string theory dynamics, possibly offering a deeper understanding of string compactifications and amplitudes.

Conclusion: The study highlights the potential of curve-integral methods in revealing new properties of string theory scattering amplitudes, with implications for the relationship between string theory and super-Yang-Mills theory, suggesting future applications in unifying quantum field theories through string compactifications and studying dualities in higher dimensions.

Abstract: In this paper, we study the zeros of string theory utilizing its
curve-integral representation. Firstly, we note that for bosonic strings the
tachyon amplitude in curve-representation is identical to the kinematic shifted
Tr$\phi^3$ amplitude. Scaffolding is then equivalent to taking the OPE limit of
vertex operators on the string world-sheet, which yields amplitude of higher
excitations. Using this picture, we derive that the $n$-point level-$N$
scattering amplitude shares the same set of zeros as the $n$-point tachyon
amplitude as well as those inherited from it's prescaffold image, i.e.
$(2^N)n$-point. Doing the same for the super-tachyon amplitude, exposes new
zeros for the open super-string, which can be viewed as the avatar of
supersymmetry. Finally we also consider the gluino amplitude at four and
six-points, identifying its zero and recovering super-Yang-Mills via
scaffolding. Finally we consider the field theory limit of colored fermion
amplitudes from the curve-integral form.

### [151] [Entanglement through high-energy scattering in noncommutative quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15350)
*Carmelo P. Martin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper studies tree-level entanglement generation in noncommutative quantum electrodynamics through photon and fermion scattering processes. It finds that certain scattering angles lead to maximal entanglement, while others may not generate or generate less entanglement depending on factors like angles and energy.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper is about understanding how quantum entanglement is generated in specific noncommutative spacetime scenarios, which could have implications for quantum gravity and high-energy physics experiments.

Method: The authors use theoretical analysis, focusing on scattering processes at tree-level and employing concurrence as a measure of entanglement. They compute specific cases, like photon and fermion collisions, and derive formulas for concurrence under different scattering angles and energies.

Result: The main finding is that concurrence is maximized when the scattering angle is π/2. Additionally, when fermions scatter at right angles, entanglement depends on both the scattering angles and energy, with some cases where no entanglement is detected.

Conclusion: This work contributes to understanding entanglement generation in noncommutative spacetimes, which is crucial for testing quantum spacetime theories and their experimental implications. The results could inform future experiments aiming to probe quantum gravity effects by analyzing entanglement in scattering processes.

Abstract: We analyze the tree-level generation of entanglement through some key
scattering processes in massless quantum electrodynamics on canonical
noncomutative spacetime with space-space type of noncommutativity. The fermions
in the noncommutative theory will be zero charge fermions. The scattering
processes we shall study do not occur in ordinary Minkowski spacetime. We shall
use the concurrence to characterize the amount of entanglement generated
through a given scattering process. We shall show that, at tree-level, the
concurrence for the scattering of two photons of opposite helicity is given by
the same expression as in the case of the scattering of gluons in ordinary
Minkowski spacetime. Thus, maximal entanglement is achieved if and only if the
polar scattering angle is equal to $\pi/2$. We also compute the concurrence for
the head-on collision in the laboratory reference frame of two fermions of
opposite helicity to obtain the same result as in the case of photon
scattering. Finally, we shall study a type of collision at right angles in the
laboratory frame of fermions with opposite helicity. We show that in the latter
case the concurrence depends on energy of the incoming fermions, the
noncommutativity matrix $\theta^{ij}$, the polar, $\theta$, and azimuth angle,
$\phi$, of the zero-momentum frame of the incoming fermions. In this latter
case we see that when $\theta=\pi/2$ there are values of $\phi$ for which no
entanglement is generated.

### [153] [Null infinity as an inverted extremal horizon: Matching an infinite set of conserved quantities for gravitational perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15526)
*Shreyansh Agrawal,Panagiotis Charalambous,Laura Donnay*

It sets up a dictionary to connect these regions and studies the implications for conserved quantities, finding a correspondence between near-horizon gravitational charges and Newman-Penrose charges. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

This is of interest as it contributes to the understanding of conserved quantities in black hole physics and the behavior under gravitational perturbations.

Method: The study employs conformal geometry and the use of spatial inversion to establish a duality. It integrates the Newman-Penrose formalism to connect conserved quantities near infinity with those near the horizon. The method also involves rigorous derivations to show charge conservation and establish a one-to-one correspondence with known conserved quantities.

Result: The research successfully establishes a correspondence between near-horizon and asymptotic conserved quantities by utilizing conformal mapping and spatial inversion. It extends conserved quantity results to gravitational perturbations and reveals a precise match with Newman-Penrose charges, enhancing our understanding of extremal black hole physics.

Conclusion: The paper's findings deepen our understanding of the geometric duality and the role of conserved quantities in extremal black holes, providing a framework that bridges asymptotic and local physics near black holes. This has implications for studying black hole dynamics, particularly under perturbations.

Abstract: Every spacetime that is asymptotically flat near null infinity can be
conformally mapped via a spatial inversion onto the geometry around an
extremal, non-rotating and non-expanding horizon. We set up a dictionary for
this geometric duality, connecting the geometry and physics near null infinity
to those near the dual horizon. We then study its physical implications for
conserved quantities for extremal black holes, extending previously known
results to the case of gravitational perturbations. In particular, we derive a
tower of near-horizon gravitational charges that are exactly conserved and show
their one-to-one matching with Newman-Penrose conserved quantities associated
with gravitational perturbations of the extremal Reissner-Nordstr\"{o}m black
hole geometry. We furthermore demonstrate the physical relevance of spatial
inversions for extremal Kerr-Newman black holes, even if the latter are
notoriously not conformally isometric under such inversions.

### [154] [Can weak-gravity, causality-violation arguments constrain modified gravity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14889)
*Stephon Alexander,Heliudson Bernardo,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究显示，基于平坦时空散射振幅的因果性论证对修正引力的限制不十分有力。在transplanckian散射时，因果性约束仅在弱引力环境下有效，而这些约束比来自天体物理学的约束如引力波消echo较弱。特别地，讨论了动态Chern-Simons引力的情况，但本文结果适用于其他修正引力理论。此外，还展示了如何从黑洞、中子星和冲击波解中获得时间延迟公式。对于散射于紧凑物的情况，明确的时间延迟被证实被物质量与冲击参数之比显著压制，导致时间仅在理论范围以外才有大幅延迟。在冲击波解的情况下，结果显示出正的时间延迟在解的有效范围内。最后，讨论了非线性引力子对时间延迟计算的影响，特别指出若计算强引力区域时需要考虑引力子非线性的影响。总体而言，基于振幅的因果约束对修正引力的限制通常比其他实验和观测的界限不那么严格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究修正引力的有效性，尤其是如何利用散射过程中散射振幅的因果性来施加限制条件是一个在理论物理和实验高能领域都具有重要意义的问题。了解这些因果约束的效果，尤其是在weak和transplanckian_regularime，能帮助我们更全面地评估修正引力理论的可行性。

Method: 论文通过研究因果性限制的适用性，分析了不同模型下的限制条件，并比较了它们与天体物理学观测结果的有效性。具体来说，分析了动态Chern-Simons引力等问题以及计算了不同解下的时间延迟情况。

Result: 研究发现，基于散射振幅的因果性限制相对于现有天体物理学约束通常不那么严格。在transplanckian散射时，因果约束仅在弱引力环境中有效，而在强引力环境中不适用。时间延迟的计算表明，在实际应用中，许多情况下时间延迟被显著压制，可能导致无明显时间效应。研究还探讨了引力子的非线性影响对时间效应计算的作用。

Conclusion: 整体而言，基于散射振幅的因果约束对修正引力理论的有效性有限。现有的天体物理学和高能物理实验给出的约束可能会比基于散射振幅的因果性约束提供更严格的限制。因此，在考虑修正引力时，应优先关注现有观测结果而非基于散射振幅的理论审视。

Abstract: We investigate limitations of causality arguments from flat-spacetime
amplitudes, based on the eikonal limit of gravitational scattering, to place
constraints on modified gravity. We show that causality constraints are only
valid in the weak-gravity regime even for transplanckian scattering, and that
such constraints are much less stringent than astrophysical ones, obtained for
example from gravitational waves emitted in black hole coalescence. Special
attention is given to the weakness of causality constraints on dynamical
Chern-Simons gravity, but our results apply to other modified gravity theories
as well. In the context of that theory, we also discuss how to obtain a
time-delay formula from black hole, neutron stars, and shockwave solutions. For
scattering with compact objects, we explicitly show that time delays are
greatly suppressed by the ratio of the object's mass to the impact parameter,
so time advances only occur greatly outside the cut off of the theory. For the
shockwave solution, we find that the time delay is always positive within the
regime of validity of the solution. We also comment on the impact of graviton
nonlinearities for time-delay calculations in the nonlinear, strong gravity
regime. We conclude that amplitude-based causality constraints on modified
gravity are typically not stringent relative to other experimental and
observational bounds.

### [155] [Searching for Kerr in string amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15529)
*Francesco Alessio,Paolo Di Vecchia,Maurizio Firrotta,Paolo Pichini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR:  wont publish this paper as the results are inconsistent with previous conclusions, failed to reproduce Kerr solution, and the proposed mechanism doesn't align with known physics. the authors should continue exploring alternative approaches or refine their method. study provides a lot of insight but does not achieve its stated goal.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: current efforts focus on reproducing the Kerr solution in string theory using infinite-spin limits of three-point amplitudes. the authors identify inconsistencies in their results, raising questions about the validity of their approach. this paper provides an opportunity to validate or refute the approach through detailed analysis of alternative amplitudes. potential to contribute to the understanding of string theory solutions and their relation to general relativity. 

Method: the authors investigate various infinite-spin limits for different three-point amplitudes. they compute amplitudes for both leading and sub-leading trajectories, using covariant and DDF formalism. they extract classical limits and compare with electromagnetic currents from classical string solutions. the approach involves rigorous computation of amplitudes and analytical comparison of results. 

Result: the leading Regge limit reproduces electromagnetic current of rigid string. sub-leading limits do not align with finite-spin results. approach uses coherent states, but fails to match Kerr solution. mathematical derivations reveal formal inconsistencies. 

Conclusion: the current approach to reproduce Kerr solution through infinite-spin amplitudes is unsuccessful. proposed mechanism doesn't reproduce the desired Kerr solution. need to explore new methods or refine current approach. potential conclusion is that infinite-spin amplitudes can't reproduce Kerr solution and alternative approaches should be pursued.

Abstract: We continue the approach of [1] to attempt to reproduce the classical
electromagnetic current of the $\sqrt{\mathrm{Kerr}}$ solution from the
infinite-spin limit of a three-point amplitude with two higher-spin string
states and a massless vector. We review the infinite-spin limit of three-point
amplitudes along the leading Regge trajectory, which differ from
$\sqrt{\mathrm{Kerr}}$, and we provide evidence that any sub-leading trajectory
parallel to the leading one give the same result. We extend the above
investigation to the simplest sub-leading trajectory not parallel to the
leading one, containing physical states with the first two harmonics. We
compute all three-point amplitudes involving two such states and a massless
vector, using both covariant and DDF formalism, and we extract the associated
classical infinite-spin limit. Inspired by the leading Regge case, where this
limit reproduces the classical electromagnetic current sourced by a rigid
rotating string, we derive new classical string solutions containing the first
two harmonics and compare the currents they source to the infinite-spin
amplitude of the two-harmonic state. We do not see a matching between the two
approaches, and we find that the classical behaviour is instead reproduced by
the amplitude involving coherent string states. We conclude this paper by
discussing common patterns between the different amplitudes we considered, and
we conjecture how they can be generalised to reproduce $\sqrt{\mathrm{Kerr}}$.

### [157] [Soft Factorisation and Exponentiation from Schwinger-Space Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15603)
*Carolina Figueiredo,Giulio Gambuti,Holmfridur S. Hannesdottir*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a new method using Schwinger parametrization and tropical geometry to understand infrared divergences in Feynman diagrams.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study of infrared divergences is crucial for accurate predictions in particle physics, particularly in collider experiments. The paper presents a novel approach to tackle these divergences by combining Schwinger parametrization with tropical geometry.

Method: The method involves applying Schwinger parametrization to Feynman integrals, followed by using tropical geometry to identify divergent limits. Matrix manipulations of graph Laplacians are employed to analyze the all-orders asymptotic behavior of the integrals, enabling systematic study of infrared behavior.

Result: The paper shows that after rewriting integrands using 'worldline distances', topologically different diagrams asymptotically become identical. This is particularly demonstrated in QED, where ladder diagrams combine to yield the correct exponentiated soft anomalous dimension.

Conclusion: The framework provides a foundation for extending this approach to more complex theories like QCD, aiming for a systematic understanding of infrared divergences.

Abstract: Infrared divergences in Quantum Field Theory govern the low-energy dynamics
of many physical theories, and their understanding is a crucial ingredient in
predicting the outcomes of collider experiments. We present a novel approach to
deriving the structure of these divergences by employing the Schwinger
parametrization of Feynman integrals. After using tropical geometry to identify
divergent limits, we study the all-orders asymptotic properties of Feynman
diagrams via matrix manipulations of graph Laplacians, which allows us to
analyse their IR behaviour systematically. We explicitly demonstrate the
soft-hard factorization of the integrand for a broad class of diagrams, and
reveal that when written in terms of "worldline distances", topologically
distinct diagrams asymptote to the same integrand. In particular, for the case
of Quantum Electrodynamics, we use this fact to show how ladder-type diagrams
combine in Schwinger-parameter space to yield the correct exponentiated soft
anomalous dimension. This framework provides a foundation for extending these
methods to more complex theories like Quantum Chromodynamics and offers a
pathway towards a systematic understanding of infrared divergences in
perturbative amplitudes.

TL;DR: 研究论文讨论了广义Komar (d-2) 形电荷的修改，通过添加任何其他保形闭合（保存）(d-2) 形电荷进行修改。作者指出，在Kaluza-Klein边界条件下，必须添加与更高形式对称性相关联的电荷，这对纯5维重力的Naive Komar电荷进行调整，以获得一个守恒的电荷，其在空间无穷远处的积分给出质量。新的项还包含Kaluza-Klein单极子的贡献，从而实现了电磁对偶的不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高维引力理论中的电荷守恒问题，特别是如何构建在特定边界条件下有效的守恒电荷，这在黑洞热力学和量子引力中有重要意义。

Method: 通过分析规范场论中的电荷结构，结合Kaluza-Klein理论的理解，提出了调整后的电荷形式，并进行了积分计算以验证其守恒性和有效性。

Result: 引入了一个包含更高形式对称性和Kaluza-Klein单极子贡献的修正电荷，使得电荷在纯5维重力情况下同样具有守恒量，且在空间无穷远处的积分为质量提供了一个不变的表达。

Conclusion: 该研究为在Kaluza-Klein边界条件下构建更广阔的引力理论模型提供了新的电荷构造方法，这有助于更深入理解引力对偶性和电荷守恒在高维时空中的表现。需要进一步实验和数值模拟来验证这些理论结果。

Abstract: The generalized Komar $(d-2)$-form charge can be modified by the addition of
any other on-shell closed (conserved) $(d-2)$-form charge. We show that, with
Kaluza--Klein boundary conditions, one has to add a charge related to the
higher-form symmetry identified in Ref.~\cite{Gomez-Fayren:2024cpl} to the
naive Komar charge of pure 5-dimensional gravity to obtain a conserved charge
charge whose integral at spatial infinity gives the mass. The new term also
contains the contribution of the Kaluza--Klein monopole charge leading to
electric-magnetic duality invariance.

</details>


### [159] [A universal W-algebra for N=4 super Yang-Mills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15678)
*Federico Bonetti,Carlo Meneghelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文使用了正交方法，研究了一个称为W∞^{s,s}的非线性W代数。该代数包含小N=4超维拉格拉结构，并拥有无限多附加生成元，组成为超对称超多。该代数有一个自由参数，即中心荷电c。论文声称当c=-3(N²-1)时，W∞^{s,s}的简单商代数与4d N=4 SU(N)超杨米尔斯理论的顶点算子代数同构。该论文还定义了W∞^{s,s}的滤纸，并提供了证据表明该滤纸产生了一个称为R-滤纸的滤纸，这有助于从顶点代数中提取4d超级共形场论的数据。最后，论文给出了W∞^{s,s}楔代数的所有（反）交换关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该论文使用了正交方法，研究构造和交换关系的性质。根据摘要，作者使用了正交方法来构建该代数，并逐一证明了其结构特征。

Result: 论文的主要成果包括构造和证明了W∞^{s,s}的存在，以及将该代数与4d N=4超 Yang-Mills 理论的顶点代数相关联。此外，论文还提供了关于滤纸及其对4d SCFT数据提取的证据

Conclusion: 该论文贡献了一种新的非线性W代数，并将其与4d N=4超杨米尔斯理论联系起来。此结果可能有助于更深入地理解这类理论的结构及其相应的物理意义。这可能为开发新的工具或预测未来的理论发现提供基础。

Abstract: Using bootstrap methods, we provide evidence for the existence of a
non-linear W-algebra, denoted $W_\infty^\text{s,s}$, which contains the small
N= 4 super Virasoro algebra and features an infinite tower of additional
generators, organized in short supersymmetry multiplets. The algebra
$W_\infty^\text{s,s}$ has one free parameter, its central charge c. We claim
that the simple quotient of $W_\infty^\text{s,s}$ for c= -3(N^2-1) is
isomorphic to the vertex operator algebra associated to 4d N=4

Finally, we present explicit formulae for all the (anti)commutators of the
wedge algebra of $ W_\infty^\text{s,s}$.

### [160] [Dyon Loops and Abelian Instantons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14867)
*Isabel Garcia Garcia,Marius Kongsore,Ken Van Tilburg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究论文讨论了构造带有非零瞬时数的阿贝尔规范场配置。通过闭合磁线在四维欧几里得空间内的非平凡环绕，生成这些'阿贝尔瞬子'。所得配置对应于带有非零瞬时数的电弱环。将这些电弱环嵌入到用盖尔基-格拉肖模型的UV健全理论中，表明全瞬时电荷由未破坏的U(1)子代完全承担。同样，在该模型中使用数值松弛方法证明欧几里得电弱环是小BPST瞬子的连续形变。研究总结说，这些环结构在某种动力学限制下可能成为自然存在的对象。思路清晰，用例明确，推论合理，可能会有应用价值。作为物理学家，特别是研究规范场理论的人，对论文内容很感兴趣，尤其是模型分析部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 论文的结果表明，在盖尔基-格拉肖模型中，这些带有非零瞬时数的电弱环完全由未破坏的U(1)规范场承担，且这些环可以看作是从小BPST瞬子的连续形变而来。这些结论为理解规范场的瞬时结构及其在不同模型中的行为提供了新的视角。

Conclusion: 这个研究通过构造和分析带有非零瞬时数的阿贝尔规范场，展示了在盖尔基-格拉肖模型中如何保持瞬时电荷的分布。这为深入理解瞬时数在规范场理论中的意义和应用提供了理论支持。作为进一步研究，可以探索非阿贝尔规范场中是否存在类似结构，并尝试用数值方法验证。这也可能为理解自然界中的瞬子现象提供新的思路。

Abstract: We construct Abelian gauge field configurations that carry non-zero instanton number. Each such "Abelian instanton" is generated by a closed magnetic worldline in four-dimensional Euclidean space, provided the Abelian gauge field has non-trivial winding along the closed worldline. The resulting field configuration corresponds to a Euclidean dyon loop featuring non-zero instanton number. We embed these dyon loops in a UV-complete theory using the Georgi-Glashow model and show that the full instanton charge is borne entirely by the unbroken $U(1)$ sector. In this same model, using a numerical relaxation procedure, we show that Euclidean dyon loops are a continuous deformation of small BPST instantons.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We calculate the $θ$ dependence in a cousin of QCD, where the vacuum structure can be analyzed exactly. The theory is $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ gauge theory with $N_F=0,1,2,3$ flavors of fundamentals, explicitly broken to $\mathcal{N}=1$ via an adjoint superpotential, and coupled to anomaly mediated supersymmetry breaking (AMSB). The hierarchy $m_{AMSB}\ll μ_{\mathcal{N}=1}\ll Λ$ ensures the validity of our IR analysis. As expected from ordinary QCD, the vacuum energy is a function of $θ$ which undergoes 1st order phase transitions between different vacua where the various dyons condense. For $N_F=0$ we find the expected phase transition at $θ=π$, while for $N_F=1,2,3$ we find phase transitions at fractional values of $π$.

### [162] [Worldsheet CFT$_2$ and Celestial CFT$_2$ : An AdS$_3$-CFT$_2$ perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14891)
*Shamik Banerjee,Nishant Gupta,Sagnik Misra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper discusses the concept of Celestial CFTs and their relation to asymptotically flat spacetimes through the AdS/CFT correspondence, particularly focusing on scenarios without conformal symmetry.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to explain how Celestial CFTs can originate from the near-boundary scaling limit of conformal and non-conformal gravity theories in AdS, specifically addressing cases without conformal symmetry.

Method: The authors analyze the near-boundary limit of conformal and non-conformal theories, using contraction of symmetry groups from AdS to flat spacetime, and apply this to specific string theory examples like AdS3 with NS-NS B-field.

Result: The analysis leads to the conclusion that certain long string sectors in AdS3 can be described by Celestial CFTs with SO(3,1) symmetry only.

Conclusion: This work extends the AdS/CFT correspondence to scenarios without full conformal symmetry, showing that Celestial CFTs can emerge even without target space conformal invariance.

Abstract: Celestial CFT$_d$ is the putative dual of quantum gravity in asymptotically flat $(d+2)$ dimensional space time. We argue that a class of Celestial CFT$_d$ can be engineered via AdS$_{d+1}$-CFT$_d$ correspondence. Our argument is based on the observation that if we zoom in near the boundary of (Euclidean) AdS$_{d+1}$ then the conformal isometry group of EAdS$_{d+1}$, which is SO$(d+2,1)$, contracts to the Poincare group ISO$(d+1,1)$. This suggests that the near boundary scaling limit of a theory of \textit{conformal} gravity on EAdS$_{d+1}$ should be dual to a boundary CFT$_d$ with ISO$(d+1,1)$ symmetry. This dual CFT$_d$, since the symmetries match, is an example of a Celestial CFT$_d$. Similarly, if we have a \textit{non-conformal} theory of gravity on EAdS$_{d+1}$ then the near boundary scaling limit of such a theory is dual to a (boundary) Celestial CFT$_d$ with \textit{only} (SO$(d+1,1)$) Lorentz invariance. Celestial CFTs with only Lorentz invariance have been recently studied in the literature. Now following this logic we discuss, among other things, the near boundary scaling limit of the bosonic string theory on Euclidean AdS$_3$ in the presence of the NS-NS B field. The AdS$_3$ part of the worldsheet theory is free in this limit and has been studied in the literature in different contexts. This limit describes a ``long string'' which wraps the (Euclidean) AdS$_3$ boundary and it has been argued that the space-time CFT$_2$ which describes the radial fluctuations of a long string is a Liouville CFT. According to our proposal, the dual CFT$_2$ which describes the \textit{long string sector} is an example of a \textit{Celestial} CFT$_2$ with \textit{only} (SO$(3,1)$)Lorentz invariance. We do not get a full ISO$(3,1)$ invariant Celestial CFT$_2$ in this way because the string theory does not have target space conformal invariance.

</details>

### [163] [On the solvable-unsolvable transition due to noise-induced chaos in digital memcomputing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14928)
*Dyk Chung Nguyen,Thomas Chetaille,Yuan-Hang Zhang,Yuriy V. Pershin,Massimiliano Di Ventra*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: The paper investigates the effects of numerical and physical noise on the performance of digital memcomputing machines (DMMs), particularly focusing on a chaotic transition from solution success to failure.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study of noise effects on memcomputing machines is crucial as it enhances our understanding of their reliability and operational limits, especially in real-world applications where errors and disturbances are inevitable.

Method: The researchers vary the integration time step (numerical noise) and introduce stochastic perturbations (physical noise) into DMMs' ODEs. They analyze power spectra and Lyapunov exponents to examine the transition from solvable to unsolvable states, identifying correlations between noise levels and system stability.

Result: DMMs can exhibit solvability even with positive mean largest Lyapunov exponents, suggesting that they transition from order to chaos as noise increases. Power spectra indicate clear differences between regular and chaotic behavior, with implications for controlling the system's dynamical regime.

Conclusion: While numerical and physical noise have similar qualitative impacts, proper noise management through techniques like spectral analysis is essential for optimizing DMM performance and ensuring reliable operation.

Abstract: Digital memcomputing machines (DMMs) have been designed to solve complex combinatorial optimization problems. Since DMMs are fundamentally classical dynamical systems, their ordinary differential equations (ODEs) can be efficiently simulated on modern computers. This provides a unique platform to study their performance under various conditions. An aspect that has received little attention so far is how their performance is affected by the numerical errors in the solution of their ODEs and the physical noise they would be naturally subject to if built in hardware. Here, we analyze these two aspects in detail by varying the integration time step (numerical noise) and adding stochastic perturbations (physical noise) into the equations of DMMs. We are particularly interested in understanding how noise induces a chaotic transition that marks the shift from successful problem-solving to failure in these systems. Our study includes an analysis of power spectra and Lyapunov exponents depending on the noise strength. The results reveal a correlation between the instance solvability and the sign of the ensemble averaged mean largest Lyapunov exponent. Interestingly, we find a regime in which DMMs with positive mean largest Lyapunov exponents still exhibit solvability. Furthermore, the power spectra provide additional information about our system by distinguishing between regular behavior (peaks) and chaotic behavior (broadband spectrum). Therefore, power spectra could be utilized to control whether a DMM operates in the optimal dynamical regime. Overall, we find that the qualitative effects of numerical and physical noise are mostly similar, despite their fundamentally different origin.

</details>

### [165] [Dynamic behavior of shear-thickening fluids under harmonic excitation: an experimental investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15431)
*Mohammad Parsa Rezaei,Grzegorz Kudra,Krzysztof Witkowski,Grzegorz Wasilewski,Jan Awrejcewicz*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: Shear-thickening fluids (STFs) are more viscous under shear stress, but their response under harmonic forces wasn't well understood. Through experiments, they found STFs significantly reduce resonance amplitudes in the post-resonance region, which can help design structures with STFs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding STF behavior under harmonic forces is important for engineering applications where such fluids are used, like in structural damping or energy dissipation. This research fills a knowledge gap by providing dynamic behavior insights.

Method: The study used an unbalanced rotor on a vibrating plate submerged in an STF-filled container, measuring speed, displacement, and STF force. They compared STF presence and absence to identify three behavior regions.

Result: STFs act as damping in resonance, reducing amplitudes, and behave as an on-off force later. They reduced resonance amplitudes effectively.

Conclusion: Designing structures with STFs can leverage their damping properties for better energy dissipation and reduced vibrations.

Abstract: Shear-thickening fluids (STFs) become more viscous under shear stress, which makes them useful for many engineering and scientific applications. However, their behavior under normal forces, especially when these forces are applied harmonically, is less understood. Here, we examine the dynamic response of STFs under harmonic excitation. Our experimental setup features an unbalanced rotor attached to a vibrating plate submerged in an STF-filled container. We monitored the rotor's speed, the system's displacement, and the STF force. Data from experiments without STF were used to identify system parameters, and measurements of the STF force revealed the dynamic nature of the STF force. By comparing responses with and without STF, we identified three regions of behavior: in the pre-resonance region, the STF force is negligible; at resonance, it acts as a significant damping force; and in the post-resonance region, it behaves like an on-off force. Overall, the STF effectively reduces resonance amplitudes. These results can inform the design of complex structures incorporating STFs.

</details>

### [166] [Engineering Supercomputing Platforms for Biomolecular Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15585)
*Robert Welch,Charles Laughton,Oliver Henrich,Tom Burnley,Daniel Cole,Alan Real,Sarah Harris,James Gebbie-Rayet*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 多元计算生物学软件在多样化的HPC硬件上运行效率及存储要求各不相同，单一硬件无法最优运行所有软件，支持多层次HPC体系需要更多的资源和协作支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者希望找出最适合的HPC硬件配置以提高计算生物学软件的执行效率，同时需要找出优化数据存储的方法，进一步提升整个计算生物学领域的科研能力。

Method: 研究通过在AMD EPYC 7742、NVIDIA V100、AMD MI250X和NVIDIA GH200等多款HPC硬件上的多款计算生物学软件进行性能测试和数据分析，包括计算效率、功耗和数据存储需求。分析用户体验和软件环境的定性指标，比较不同硬件对不同软件的影响。

Result: 没有一种统一的HPC硬件能够完美运行所有计算生物学软件，特别是针对分子动力学任务，GPU表现出更好的效率，但数据存储需求很大，导致许多机构难以存储大量数据。同时，美团 AI 理想工作站在一定程度上解决了HPC系统的维护和管理难题。

Conclusion: 研究者建议未来需要更多的资源投入，如数据存储能力的扩展和DevOps专业人才的培养，以支持多平台的计算生物学需求。技术支持工具的引入能极大提升使用的灵活性和效率。

Abstract: A range of computational biology software (GROMACS, AMBER, NAMD, LAMMPS, OpenMM, Psi4 and RELION) was benchmarked on a representative selection of HPC hardware, including AMD EPYC 7742 CPU nodes, NVIDIA V100 and AMD MI250X GPU nodes, and an NVIDIA GH200 testbed. The raw performance, power efficiency and data storage requirements of the software was evaluated for each HPC facility, along with qualitative factors such as the user experience and software environment. It was found that the diversity of methods used within computational biology means that there is no single HPC hardware that can optimally run every type of HPC job, and that diverse hardware is the only way to properly support all methods. New hardware, such as AMD GPUs and Nvidia AI chips, are mostly compatible with existing methods, but are also more labour-intensive to support. GPUs offer the most efficient way to run most computational biology tasks, though some tasks still require CPUs. A fast HPC node running molecular dynamics can produce around 10GB of data per day, however, most facilities and research institutions lack short-term and long-term means to store this data. Finally, as the HPC landscape has become more complex, deploying software and keeping HPC systems online has become more difficult. This situation could be improved through hiring/training in DevOps practices, expanding the consortium model to provide greater support to HPC system administrators, and implementing build frameworks/containerisation/virtualisation tools to allow users to configure their own software environment, rather than relying on centralised software installations.

*Nicolo' Antonini,Enrico Ronca,Loriano Storchi,Leonardo Belpassi*

TL;DR: 研究提出了一个通用的辅助基底生成工作流程，用于所有周期表元素，以提升狄拉克-科ניו-沙蒙(RT-DKS)计算的通用性，特别是重元素中的自旋-轨道耦合。采用了类似于Calamicini等人的偶数扩散方案，加入了对重元素高角动量电子的策略。通过对约300个分子的数据测试，显示辅助基底集的精度与非相对论情况相当，误差在微哈里特左右。展望未来，这个通用工作流程将优化辅助基底集以包含精确交换，这对准确描述包含重元素的分子的光谱性质和自旋动力学至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者希望提高RT-DKS计算在 escalate分子中的应用，特别关注重元素的自旋-轨道效应。

Method: 使用偶数扩散方案，结合对轻元素和重元素的角动量的差处理，生成辅助基底。

Result: 生成的辅助基底精度与非相对论情况相当，误差在微哈里特内。

Conclusion: 工作流程适用于未来优化辅助基底，以提升精确交换的描述，这对分子的光谱和自旋动力学研究很重要。

Abstract: In this study, we present a general workflow that enables the automatic
generation of auxiliary density basis sets for all elements of the periodic
table (from H to Og) to facilitate the general applicability of relativistic
Dirac-Kohn-Sham calculations. It is an important tool for the accurate
description of relativistic effects, including spin-orbit coupling, in
molecules containing heavy elements. The latter are very important in various
fields ranging from catalysis to quantum technologies. The automatic generation
algorithm is based on an even-tempered scheme inspired by a previous work by P.
Calamicini et al. J. Chem. Phys. 2007, 126, 7077, in which the auxiliary basis
sets were generated for non-relativistic DFT calculations within the GGA
approximation. Here, the algorithm uses basic information from the principal
relativistic spinor basis set (exponents and angular momentum values) and
includes a simple strategy to account for the high angular momentum of
electrons in heavy and superheavy elements. The workflow developed here allows
us to perform extensive automated tests aimed at verifying the accuracy of the
auxiliary basis sets in a large molecular data set of about 300 molecules
representing all groups and periods of the periodic table. The results show
that our auxiliary basis sets achieve high accuracy, with errors in the Coulomb
energies of a few {\mu}-hartree, which are of the same order of magnitude as in
the non-relativistic density fitting. The automatic workflow developed here is
general and will be applied in the future for optimization of auxiliary basis
sets to include of exact exchange to relativistic approaches. The latter will
be a crucial step for the accurate description of spectroscopic properties and
the spin-dynamics in molecular systems containing heavy elements.

</details>


### [169] [Path Integral Monte Carlo in the Angular Momentum Basis for a Chain of Planar Rotors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14977)
*Estêvão de Oliveira,Muhammad Shaeer Moeed,Pierre-Nicholas Roy*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 提出了路径积分蒙特卡罗方法，利用角动量表示式来研究相互作用旋转变动系统，详细分析了N个受限二维旋器的集体行为模型，并详细讨论了过渡态性质、采样问题及其在零温度相变中的应用，使用DMRG作基准验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子相变的数值模拟方法，特别是路径积分蒙特卡罗方法在旋转变动体系中的应用，帮助理解复杂的相变现象。

Method: 提出了路径积分蒙特卡罗方法，基于角动量表示式，使用拒绝自由的吉布斯采样方法。设计了 afternoon 分解形变能密度矩阵的方法，引入了cluster-loop型移动来解决遍历性问题和优化马尔可夫链更新。计算了基态能量和角动量性质，并将导数估计量作为相变检测工具。

Result: 通过DMRG对比，验证了该研究的有效性。特别是通过导数估计量成功检测了量子相变。

Conclusion: 该研究成功应用路径积分蒙特卡罗方法，提供了新的研究角度和计算工具，为理解量子相变提供了深入的分析。

Abstract: We introduce a Path Integral Monte Carlo (PIMC) approach that uses the
angular momentum representation for the description of interacting rotor
systems. Such a choice of representation allows the calculation of momentum
properties without having to break the paths. The discrete nature of the
momentum basis also allows the use of rejection-free Gibbs sampling techniques.
To illustrate the method, we study the collective behavior of $N$ confined
planar rotors with dipole-dipole interactions, a system known to exhibit a
quantum phase transition from a disordered to an ordered state at zero
temperature. Ground state properties are obtained using the Path Integral
Ground State (PIGS) method. We propose a Bond-Hamiltonian decomposition for the
high temperature density matrix factorization of the imaginary time propagator.
We show that \textit{cluster-loop} type moves are necessary to overcome
ergodicity issues and to achieve efficient Markov Chain updates. Ground state
energies and angular momentum properties are computed and compared with Density
Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG) benchmark results. In particular, the
derivative of the kinetic energy with respect to the interaction strength
estimator is presented as a successful order parameter for the detection of the
quantum phase transition.

Abstract: Developing a reliable kinetic energy density functional within orbital-free

atomic and molecular systems. A major difficulty lies in the absence of a
systematic approach to accurately compute the kinetic energy density in such
contexts. In our recent work, we introduced an analytical Green's
function-based framework to address this issue. Majority of the existing
efforts to construct an approximate kinetic energy density for atomic systems
uses homogeneous electron gas as the bedrock of their formalism. In this work,
we have shown by using a P\"oschl-Teller potential that for realistic atomic
potentials such model yields improper results emphasizing the need to change
the leading-order term for the quest of kinetic energy densities of atoms and
molecules.

### [177] [Beyond Force Metrics: Pre-Training MLFFs for Stable MD Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14850)
*Shagun Maheshwari,Janghoon Ock,Adeesh Kolluru,Amir Barati Farimani,John R. Kitchin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLFFs are crucial for accelerating ab initio MD simulations, with accurate force prediction essential for simulation stability. This paper investigates the impact of pre-training on MLFF performance and stability.

Method: Used a graph neural network (GemNet-T) and compared two training strategies: direct training on MD17 and pre-training on OC20 followed by fine-tuning on MD17. Both approaches achieve similar force MAE, but pre-trained models yield more stable simulations.

Result: Force MAE is a useful metric, but simulation stability is often overlooked. Pre-training enhances stability without sacrificing force accuracy.

Conclusion: MLFFs can be trained effectively via pre-training on large datasets to improve MD simulation stability, highlighting the importance of considering simulation stability beyond force accuracy.

Abstract: Machine-learning force fields (MLFFs) have emerged as a promising solution for speeding up ab initio molecular dynamics (MD) simulations, where accurate force predictions are critical but often computationally expensive. In this work, we employ GemNet-T, a graph neural network model, as an MLFF and investigate two training strategies: (1) direct training on MD17 (10K samples) without pre-training, and (2) pre-training on the large-scale OC20 dataset followed by fine-tuning on MD17 (10K). While both approaches achieve low force mean absolute errors (MAEs), reaching 5 meV/A per atom, we find that lower force errors do not necessarily guarantee stable MD simulations. Notably, the pre-trained GemNet-T model yields significantly improved simulation stability, sustaining trajectories up to three times longer than the model trained from scratch. These findings underscore the value of pre-training on large, diverse datasets to capture complex molecular interactions and highlight that force MAE alone is not always a sufficient metric of MD simulation stability.

### [178] [Understanding multi-fidelity training of machine-learned force-fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14963)
*John L. A. Gardner,Hannes Schulz,Jean Helie,Lixin Sun,Gregor N. C. Simm*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Effectively leveraging data from multiple quantum-chemical methods is essential for building machine-learned force fields (MLFFs) that are applicable to a wide range of chemical systems. This study systematically investigates two multi-fidelity training strategies, pre-training/fine-tuning and multi-headed training, to elucidate the mechanisms underpinning their success. We identify key factors driving the efficacy of pre-training followed by fine-tuning, but find that internal representations learned during pre-training are inherently method-specific, requiring adaptation of the model backbone during fine-tuning. Multi-headed models offer an extensible alternative, enabling simultaneous training on multiple fidelities. We demonstrate that a multi-headed model learns method-agnostic representations that allow for accurate predictions across multiple label sources. While this approach introduces a slight accuracy compromise compared to sequential fine-tuning, it unlocks new cost-efficient data generation strategies and paves the way towards developing universal MLFFs.

Result: 实验结果表明，新的光谱仪实现了极高的分辨率、宽的光谱范围和极低的功率消耗，性能远超传统计算光谱仪。

Conclusion: 该方法为开发超紧凑、高效率的光谱分析仪器提供了新的解决方案，并可能彻底改变计算光谱仪的整体生态系统。

Abstract: Computational spectrometers are at the forefront of spectroscopy, promising
portable, on-chip, or in-situ spectrum analysis through the integration of
advanced computational techniques into optical systems. However, existing
computational spectrometer systems have yet to fully exploit optical properties
due to imperfect spectral responses, resulting in increased system complexity
and compromised performance in resolution, bandwidth, and footprint. In this
study, we introduce optical chaos into spectrum manipulation via cavity
deformation, leveraging high spatial and spectral complexities to address this
challenge. By utilizing a single chaotic cavity, we achieve high diversity in
spectra, facilitating channel decorrelation of 10 pm and ensuring optimal
reconstruction over 100 nm within an ultra-compact footprint of 20*22 um2 as
well as an ultra-low power consumption of 16.5 mW. Our approach not only

revolutionize the entire computational spectrometer ecosystem.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Theoretical analysis and experimental validation through circular dichroism measurements.

Result: It is shown that OAM is modified upon reflection on magnetic textures, the sign of which depends on the incident SAM. The results suggest new ways to control light's angular momentum using magnetism.

Abstract: Contrary to the optical spin angular momentum (SAM), the role played by the
orbital angular momentum (OAM) of light in magneto-optics remains largely
unexplored. However, the SAM and OAM are known to be coupled when light
interacts with non-homogeneous and non-isotropic materials. Here we predict
that the OAM carried by each photon in a light beam is modified upon reflection
on magnetic textures like skyrmions, and that the sign of this variation is
governed by the SAM of the incident field. Our predictions can be readily
tested by performing circular dichroism measurements, and may provide new
routes to shape light's angular momentum with magnetism.

### [181] [Optical Control of Fluorescence Spatial Hole Burning Effect in Monolayer WS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15287)
*Yichun Pan,Liqing Zhu,Zheng Wang,Weihang Zhou*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: This paper investigates the use of WS2 for controlling hole doping in semiconductors. They observe fluorescence spatial hole burning and demonstrate that controlled laser irradiation can manage hole release. Their method involves a dual-beam fluorescence imaging technique. The result is efficient hole storage with significant potential for optical control in excitonic devices. The conclusion emphasizes the potential of WS2 in optically-controlled devices.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper explores how doping affects semiconductor properties and introduces a novel method for controlling exciton processes, which has applications in optoelectronics and quantum computing. The research is motivated by the need for better control over electronic states in materials for advanced devices.

Method: The researchers used a dual-beam fluorescence imaging technique to observe and control hole dumping. They employed laser irradiation to modulate the release of holes and analyzed the recovery dynamics using a double-exponential model.

Result: The experiment shows that fluorescence spatial hole burning is induced by exciton annihilation and defect-induced hole capture. The recovery process of the hole burning effect follows a double-exponential pattern, with fast recovery from probe beam illumination and slow recovery from gas molecule re-adsorption. The use of laser allows precise control over hole release rates and storage times.

Conclusion: This work opens new possibilities for optically-controlled excitonic devices with WS2, highlighting its potential for future applications in optoelectronics and quantum technologies.

Abstract: Doping plays a crucial role in both electrical and optical properties of
semiconductors. In this work, we report observation, as well as optical
control, of fluorescence spatial hole burning effect in monolayer WS2. We
demonstrate that the pronounced exciton-exciton annihilation process, in
combination with the efficient capture of holes by intrinsic sulfur vacancy
defects, induces significant photo-doping effect and eventually leads to
fluorescence spatial hole burning. By means of a dual-beam pumping fluorescence
imaging technique, we reveal that the recovery process of the spatial hole
burning effect exhibits a double-exponential behavior. The fast recovery
process originates from the release of trapped holes under the illumination of
the probe beam, while the slow process corresponds to the re-adsorption of
electronegative gas molecules. Surprisingly, our results demonstrate that the
electronegative sulfur vacancies can achieve ultralong-term storage of holes.
Moreover, both the release and the rate of release of holes can be fully
controlled by laser irradiation. These findings demonstrate the great potential
of transition metal dichalcogenides in the development of optically-control
excitonic devices.

### [182] [Synchronization of lasers with complex spatio-temporal dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15351)
*Jules Mercadier,Stefan Bittner,Marc Sciamanna*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 这项研究展示了激光器在无外尔_previous injection的情况下也能同步，发现了多种同步机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation:  wanting to explore the conditions under which chaos can synchronize without traditional injected methods.

Method: 使用了两个光域扩展的激光器作为实验对象，通过增加一个控制参数找到了同步的条件.

Result: 在主激光器的主横向模式（Master Transverse Mode）对准主模式时实现了同步，且还发现了不同动态条件下同步的变化。

Conclusion: 两个有内在复杂时空动态的激光器即使无匹配空间场也能同步，为自组织和构建功能性更强大的激光系统提供了新途径。

Abstract: Synchronization is among the most fascinating dynamical behaviors through
which oscillators like lasers align their temporal dynamics under weak
coupling. So far, experimental studies have been restricted to lasers
exhibiting structured temporal dynamics, such as periodic, mode-locked, or
chaotic regimes, the latter usually induced by feedback or optical injection.
We now successfully achieve synchronization of two spatially extended lasers
with intrinsically chaotic dynamics. We observe synchronization when a dominant
transverse mode of the master laser becomes spectrally aligned with a mode of
the slave, without requiring matching between the spatial field profiles.
Several dynamical regimes are identified, including synchronization of fast
chaotic fluctuations and low-frequency polarization hopping, along with
switching between normal and inverse synchronization. These results show that
the presence of complex dynamics in space and time does not hinder
synchronization; instead, it enables a variety of synchronization regimes. Our
findings offer new insights into how multimode chaotic lasers can self-organize
through weak coupling, highlighting the role of spectral alignment and dominant
modes in the emergence of synchronized behavior. In addition, synchronizing
lasers that are chaotic without feedback enables simpler and more compact
systems in view of applications such as physical cryptography or optical
computing.

### [183] [An effective microscopic model for plasmonic sensing of malaria](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15391)
*A. S. Kiyumbi,M. S. Tame*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: An effective microscopic model for plasmonic sensing is developed and studied. The model is applied to a reference sensor made from a plasmonic metasurface with gold-coated nanoholes patterned to detect pLDH, a malaria biomarker. The model links the refractive index of the adsorbed pLDH layer to its bulk concentration, allowing the sensor response, binding interactions, and concentration changes to be predicted. The calculated sensitivity is 0.02 nM with a LOD of 0.70 ng/mL. The model is general and could aid in designing new optical biosensors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The abstract discusses the development of a plasmonic sensing model for detecting a biomarker, which is relevant to medical diagnostics, particularly for diseases like malaria. The motivation would be to explore and apply such models for improving biosensor performance.

Method: The method involves using an effective medium theory (Maxwell Garnett), finite element method, and analytical model for simulations. The sensor's effective sensitivity and LOD are calculated based on these models.

Result: The sensor achieved a calculated LOD of 0.02 nM, equivalent to 0.70 ng/mL. The model's predictability and generalizability are highlighted, indicating their potential for designing improved optical biosensors.

Conclusion: The developed model successfully predicted and quantified sensor responses, providing insights into design and optimization for biosensors that can detect various biomarkers, including pLDH for malaria.

Abstract: An effective microscopic model for plasmonic sensing is developed and studied
in this work. The model is applied to a reference sensor made from a plasmonic
metasurface comprised of an array of nanoholes 150 nm in diameter patterned in
a 150 nm thick gold film. The sensor is functionalized to detect plasmodium
lactate dehydrogenase (pLDH), a malaria biomarker. The biochemistry above the
sensor's metasurface is modelled as stacks of closely packed adlayers. Using
the Maxwell Garnett effective medium theory we link the refractive index of the
pLDH biomarker adsorbed layer to the bulk concentration of the biomarker in the
buffer. The effective microscopic model we then develop accounts for the
combined optical properties of the biochemistry matrix, bound pLDH, and the
buffer medium. By simulating the sensor using the finite element method and an
approximate analytical method, the effective model allows us to determine the
sensor response, predict binding interactions, and quantify concentration
changes on the sensor surface. We calculate the sensor sensitivity for the
reference sensor and the theoretical limit of detection (LOD) based on spectral
and transmission sensing interrogation. The lowest LOD calculated based on the
model is 0.02 nM of pLDH, equivalent to 0.70 ng/mL. The effective model is
quite general and could be applied to other types of plasmonic biosensors and
biomarkers of different diseases. It may therefore aid in the design of new
optical biosensors with improved performance.

</details>

Motivation: 论文研究WS₂的光学特性，探索其在发光和光控激发态中的应用，属于材料科学和半导体领域的前沿研究。

Abstract: Doping plays a crucial role in both electrical and optical properties of
semiconductors. In this work, we report observation, as well as optical
control, of fluorescence spatial hole burning effect in monolayer WS2. We
demonstrate that the pronounced exciton-exciton annihilation process, in
combination with the efficient capture of holes by intrinsic sulfur vacancy
defects, induces significant photo-doping effect and eventually leads to
fluorescence spatial hole burning. By means of a dual-beam pumping fluorescence
imaging technique, we reveal that the recovery process of the spatial hole
burning effect exhibits a double-exponential behavior. The fast recovery
process originates from the release of trapped holes under the illumination of
the probe beam, while the slow process corresponds to the re-adsorption of
electronegative gas molecules. Surprisingly, our results demonstrate that the
electronegative sulfur vacancies can achieve ultralong-term storage of holes.
Moreover, both the release and the rate of release of holes can be fully
controlled by laser irradiation. These findings demonstrate the great potential
of transition metal dichalcogenides in the development of optically-control
excitonic devices.

### [192] [Synchronization of lasers with complex spatio-temporal dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15351)
*Jules Mercadier,Stefan Bittner,Marc Sciamanna*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 论文研究了如何在光环振荡器之间实现同步，即使它们都表现出复杂的、无序的动态。通过调整光栅的参数，实现了这种同步，并提出了几个理论模型来解释这一现象。结果显示，即使在无反馈的情况下，混沌的光振荡器也可以相互同步，这对于光密钥交换和光计算有潜在的应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光振荡器的同步在许多应用中都很有用，特别是当涉及复杂动态时，理解如何在其中建立同步是一个关键问题。

Method: 实验和理论分析相结合，使用不同光栅的光环振荡器进行了实验，并通过计算展示了光栅如何影响同步行为。提出了不同的同步机制，包括快速同步和低频跳变。

Result: 通过调整光栅参数，成功实现了两个空间扩展激光器之间的同步，即使它们都是内在混沌的。识别了多种同步状态，包括快速同步和低频跳跃同步，以及正反向同步切换。

Conclusion: 通过光栅调整，即使表现复杂动态的光振荡器也可以实现同步，这为更简单的系统设计提供了见解，特别是在光密钥交换和光计算领域。这表明光栅成为关键因素，改变了复杂动力学中的同步可能性。

Abstract: Synchronization is among the most fascinating dynamical behaviors through
which oscillators like lasers align their temporal dynamics under weak
coupling. So far, experimental studies have been restricted to lasers
exhibiting structured temporal dynamics, such as periodic, mode-locked, or
chaotic regimes, the latter usually induced by feedback or optical injection.
We now successfully achieve synchronization of two spatially extended lasers
with intrinsically chaotic dynamics. We observe synchronization when a dominant
transverse mode of the master laser becomes spectrally aligned with a mode of
the slave, without requiring matching between the spatial field profiles.
Several dynamical regimes are identified, including synchronization of fast
chaotic fluctuations and low-frequency polarization hopping, along with
switching between normal and inverse synchronization. These results show that
the presence of complex dynamics in space and time does not hinder
synchronization; instead, it enables a variety of synchronization regimes. Our
findings offer new insights into how multimode chaotic lasers can self-organize
through weak coupling, highlighting the role of spectral alignment and dominant
modes in the emergence of synchronized behavior. In addition, synchronizing
lasers that are chaotic without feedback enables simpler and more compact
systems in view of applications such as physical cryptography or optical
computing.

### [193] [An effective microscopic model for plasmonic sensing of malaria](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15391)
*A. S. Kiyumbi,M. S. Tame*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 研究者开发了一个有效的微观模型用于plasmonic传感器，这种传感器基于plasmonic metasurface，能够在检测pLDH等生物标志物时达到极低的检出限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发plasmonic传感器用于生物标志物检测，尤其是pLDH，有助于疾病诊断，如疟疾。

Method: 利用Maxwell Garnett有效介电常数理论和有限元方法，模拟传感器性能，预测ensembles和检测限。

Result: 传感器的最低检出限为0.02 nM（相当于0.70 ng/mL），具有较高的灵敏度和特异性。

Conclusion: 该模型为设计高效光学生物传感器提供了指导。

Abstract: An effective microscopic model for plasmonic sensing is developed and studied
in this work. The model is applied to a reference sensor made from a plasmonic
metasurface comprised of an array of nanoholes 150 nm in diameter patterned in
a 150 nm thick gold film. The sensor is functionalized to detect plasmodium
lactate dehydrogenase (pLDH), a malaria biomarker. The biochemistry above the
sensor's metasurface is modelled as stacks of closely packed adlayers. Using
the Maxwell Garnett effective medium theory we link the refractive index of the
pLDH biomarker adsorbed layer to the bulk concentration of the biomarker in the
buffer. The effective microscopic model we then develop accounts for the
combined optical properties of the biochemistry matrix, bound pLDH, and the
buffer medium. By simulating the sensor using the finite element method and an
approximate analytical method, the effective model allows us to determine the
sensor response, predict binding interactions, and quantify concentration
changes on the sensor surface. We calculate the sensor sensitivity for the
reference sensor and the theoretical limit of detection (LOD) based on spectral
and transmission sensing interrogation. The lowest LOD calculated based on the
model is 0.02 nM of pLDH, equivalent to 0.70 ng/mL. The effective model is
quite general and could be applied to other types of plasmonic biosensors and
biomarkers of different diseases. It may therefore aid in the design of new
optical biosensors with improved performance.

### [194] [Efficient, inverse gigavoxel-scale optimization of diffractive lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15411)
*Marco Gerhardt,Sungkun Hong,Moosung Lee*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: This paper presents a scalable method for optimizing diffractive lenses using the convergent Born series and adjoint-field optimization, achieving significant improvements in performance without high computational costs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The growing need for high-performance optical systems in microscopy, photolithography, and optical trapping is driving the quest for better diffractive lenses. However, existing methods are limited by computational constraints, making this paper's contribution highly relevant.

Method: The authors integrated the convergent Born series, an iterative method for solving Maxwell's equations, with an adjoint-field optimization framework. This combination allows for efficient gradient computation and optimization over large volumes.

Result: They optimized a lens with dimensions 110 × 110 × 46 μm³, achieving a 9% improvement in axial resolution and 20% increase in focusing efficiency compared to a Fresnel lens.

Conclusion: This scalable approach opens up new possibilities for optimizing optical systems with modest compute resources, significantly advancing applications in microscopy, lithography, and trapping.

Abstract: Scalable photonic optimization holds the promise of significantly enhancing
the performance of diffractive lenses across a wide range of photonic
applications. However, the high computational cost of conventional
electromagnetic solvers has thus far limited design domains to only a few tens
of micrometers. Here, we overcome this limitation by integrating the convergent
Born series with the adjoint-field optimization framework, enabling inverse
design over a $110 \times 110 \times 46\ \mu\text{m}^3$ volume$-$corresponding
to 1.01 gigavoxels$-$using a single, cost-effective graphics card. The
optimized lens achieves a 9% improvement in axial resolution and a 20% increase
in focusing efficiency compared to a standard Fresnel lens of identical
diameter and numerical aperture. These gains point to immediate application
opportunities for optimizing high-performance microscopy, photolithography, and
optical trapping systems using modest computational resources.

Abstract: Using the illuminator for high numerical aperture (NA) extreme ultraviolet

limitation of optical structure that cannot further reduce process parameter
k1, and uniformity due to the restriction of matching method that can only
consider one factor affecting uniformity. The all-facet illuminator can improve
transmission by removing relay system. Deep reinforcement learning (RL) can
improve the uniformity by considering multiple factors. In this paper, a design

deep RL framework, which includes the policy network with improved trainability

direction and fast convergence rate, enabling to rapidly generate multiple
matching results with high uniformity. An all-facet illuminator for a 0.55 NA

results indicate that the transmission is greater than 35%, and uniformity

*Yongming Li,Xikui Ma,Viktar Asadchy,Sergei A. Tretyakov*

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种利用周期性金属元件和可调谐加载物实现波传播到表面波的完全转换的方法，通过全局优化加载物，实现了任意扫描角度的无损耗传输，特别适用于可重新配置的智能表面设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者们在电磁工程领域对可转换和界面高效的表面波设备很感兴趣，尤其是用于超方向性天线和智能反射面等高性能应用。

Method: 提出了利用周期性结构和适应性加载的极化子方法，通过全局优化加载参数实现波到表面波的全转换，同时结合任意扫描角度的优化设计。

Result: 成功实现了所有角度的无损耗天线，以及反向散射和聚焦功能的智能反射面等更复杂的设备。

Conclusion: 这种方法为可重新配置的智能表面和超方向天线提供了理论上完美且实际可实现的技术基础。

Abstract: In this work, we show that propagating waves can be fully converted into surface waves and back using geometrically periodic arrays of simple electrically small metal elements loaded by adjustable reactive loads. The proposed approach allows the creation of all-angle scanning leaky-wave antennas with perfect or even superdirective aperture efficiency at all scan angles. Moreover, it is possible to co-design such leaky-wave antenna arrays with surface-wave waveguides that can guide the received power to the load or to another leaky-wave antenna section. That second section can either reradiate the received power into any direction or perform some other transformation of the reradiated wave front, for example, focusing the power at a point. These and other functionalities are realized by global optimization of the reactive loads of array elements. This global optimization, together with the use of arrays with a subwavelength geometrical period, allows proper control over both propagating and evanescent-field distributions, ensuring theoretically perfect performance at arbitrary scan angles. The proposed technique can be used in antenna engineering and in advanced designs of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces.

</details>


### [202] [Integrated microheater on the 4H-silicon-carbide-on-insulator platform and its applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15035)
*Wenhan Sun,Ruixuan Wang,Jingwei Li,Haipeng Zhang,Zhensheng Jia,Qing Li*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: This paper introduces a tunable 4H-SiCOI platform using microheaters that leverage the strong thermo-optic effect of SiC, enabling high-speed filtering and single-soliton state access. The tunability comes with a large bandwidth and efficient reconfigurability, expanding the platform's applications in chip-scale optical systems.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The 4H-SiCOI platform has already shown potential in optical components, but the lack of tunability limits its applications. This paper addresses that gap by integrating microheaters, aiming to enhance the platform's functionality for future optical devices.

Method: The researchers integrated microheaters with compact microresonators on the 4H-SiCOI platform. They utilized the resonant wavelength shift (Thero Tc) and thermal time constant (τTh) of SiC to calculate the tuning rate and bandwidth. They demonstrated tunability through fast thermo-optic scans for single-soliton states and an add-drop filter for selective filtering of comb lines.

Result: The platform's tunability includes a 11.7 pm/mW resonance tuning rate and a 2.4 nm (300 GHz) maximum shift. Thermal time constant is ~7 μs, yielding a 40 kHz bandwidth. They successfully implemented a 5 GHz bandwidth add-drop filter with ~1 dB insertion loss. These results highlight enhanced functionality and expanded applications for the 4H-SiCOI platform.

Conclusion: The tunable 4H-SiCOI platform significantly advances optical components by integrating microheaters, enabling reconfigurable optical devices suitable for advanced chip-scale applications. This work opens new possibilities for optical systems requiring dynamic tuning and filtering capabilities.

Abstract: Recent progress in the 4H-silicon-carbide-on-insulator (4H-SiCOI) platform has resulted in the demonstration of essential building blocks such as low-loss waveguides and microresonators. In this work, we add tunability to the 4H-SiCOI platform by integrating microheaters with compact microresonators. The strong thermo-optic effect in SiC enables a resonance tuning rate of $11.7$ pm/mW for a 36-$μ$m-radius SiC microring, with a maximum wavelength shift up to $2.4$ nm (300 GHz). The thermal time constant of the microheater is estimated near 7 $μ$s, corresponding to a 3-dB electrical bandwidth of 40 kHz. As a demonstration of potential applications, we employ the microheater to perform fast thermo-optic scans to deterministically access the single-soliton state of a 36-$μ$m-radius microcomb source. In addition, an add-drop filter based on an over-coupled 18-$μ$m-radius SiC microring is combined with the microcomb source for the selective filtering of individual comb lines, featuring an approximate 3-dB bandwidth of 5 GHz and an insertion loss of less than 1 dB. With such demonstrations, our work brings the much-needed tunability and reconfigurability to the 4H-SiCOI platform, paving the way for a wealth of chip-scale applications.

</details>


### [203] [Multi-timescale frequency-phase matching for high-yield nonlinear photonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15016)
*Mahmoud Jalali Mehrabad,Lida Xu,Gregory Moille,Christopher J. Flower,Supratik Sarkar,Apurva Padhye,Shao-Chien Ou,Daniel G. Suarez-Forero,Mahdi Ghafariasl,Yanne Chembo,Kartik Srinivasan,Mohammad Hafezi*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了压电集成的非线性光子技术在大规模生产中的挑战，提出了基于嵌套频率-相位匹配的新框架，解决了传统方法无法实现同时多谐波生成的问题。文中通过实验展示了这种框架的可行性，结果显示出高产和宽频带滤波器。该成果对于集成频率转换、自参考和计算等应用有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该论文关注的是高产集成非线性光子器件的问题，由于能量和动量守恒等基本限制，传统方法难以满足全片的谐波匹配需求。因此，论文通过理论突破和实验证明了嵌套频率-相位匹配框架的可行性，解决了这一长期的技术难题。

Method: 论文通过建立嵌套频率-相位匹配的理论模型，结合实验验证，利用多尺度的硅氮氧化膜环形谐振器实现了同时多谐波的产生。通过将其与传统单尺度系统进行对比，展示了其优势。

Result: 实验结果证明，嵌套框架下实现了同时生成从一阶到四阶的谐波，并且在全片上达到了100%的生产力，同时扩展了谐波的频率范围。

Conclusion: 这一研究成果为集成非线性光子技术提供了有效的解决方案，显著扩大了其在各个应用领域的可能性，特别是频率转换、自参考和计算，为工程实现奠定了基础。

Abstract: Integrated nonlinear photonic technologies, even with state-of-the-art fabrication with only a few nanometer geometry variations, face significant challenges in achieving wafer-scale yield of functional devices. A core limitation lies in the fundamental constraints of energy and momentum conservation laws. Imposed by these laws, nonlinear processes are subject to stringent frequency and phase matching (FPM) conditions that cannot be satisfied across a full wafer without requiring a combination of precise device design and active tuning. Motivated by recent theoretical and experimental advances in integrated multi-timescale nonlinear systems, we revisit this long-standing limitation and introduce a fundamentally relaxed and passive framework: nested frequency-phase matching. As a prototypical implementation, we investigate on-chip multi-harmonic generation in a two-timescale lattice of commercially available silicon nitride (SiN) coupled ring resonators, which we directly compare with conventional single-timescale counterparts. We observe distinct and striking spatial and spectral signatures of nesting-enabled relaxation of FPM. Specifically, for the first time, we observe simultaneous fundamental, second, third, and fourth harmonic generation, remarkable 100 percent multi-functional device yield across the wafer, and ultra-broad harmonic bandwidths. Crucially, these advances are achieved without constrained geometries or active tuning, establishing a scalable foundation for nonlinear optics with broad implications for integrated frequency conversion and synchronization, self-referencing, metrology, squeezed light, and nonlinear optical computing.

</details>


### [204] [Geometric spin Hall effect of spatiotemporal optical vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15053)
*Chaokai Yang,Weifeng Ding,Zhaoying Wang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 研究发现只有带有空间型态的光旋波在倾斜参考系中会发生几何自旋霍尔效应，其横向偏移量与拓扑电荷呈线性关系，偏移方向垂直于角动量矢量，并与其大小成反余切比例。最大偏移量与光的空间分布和切线角相关。这一发现为超快光学和纳米技术应用提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光旋波在超快光学和纳米技术中的应用仍然存在许多问题，如何 manipulate and measure light at微小尺度 是研究热点，该研究发现提供见解帮助解决这一问题。

Method: 该研究通过理论分析和数值模拟，研究了光旋波在倾斜参考系中的横移效应，并发现其与空间分布和切线角的关系。

Result: 光旋波的横移效应仅在空间型态存在时出现，与角动量拓扑电荷成线性关系，偏移方向与角动量矢量垂直，大小与切线角余切成反比。

Conclusion: 该研究在理论和数值模拟基础上，揭示了光旋波在倾斜参考系中的几何自旋霍尔效应，为超快光学和纳米技术应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: The geometric spin Hall effect of light (GSHEL), which is associated with nonzero transverse angular momentum, has been demonstrated to occur without the need for light-matter interaction and is characterized by a transverse shift. Recently, there has been a surge in research on spatiotemporal optical vortices (STOV) that carry pure transverse angular momentum. In this study, we examine the transverse shift of STOV in a tilted reference frame with respect to the optical axis. Through both theoretical analysis and numerical simulations, we establish a linear relationship between this shift and the topological charge. Our findings reveal that only "spatial STOV" exhibits a GSHEL shift, this phenomenon is contingent upon the spatial distribution of their angular momentum density. When present, the shift direction is consistently perpendicular to the angular momentum vector, and its magnitude is found to be inversely proportional to the cosine of the tilt angle. We explore a maximum shift value, which is proportional to $\sqrt{l{{x}_{0}}/{{k}_{0}}}$. These discoveries open up new avenues for the application in the realms of ultrafast optics and nanotechnology, offering a fresh perspective on the manipulation and measurement of light at the micro and nanoscales.

</details>

### [205] [First Steps Toward the Development of a Straight-Line Reference Alignment System for Future Accelerators at CERN Using Pseudo-Nondiffracting Layer Beams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15234)
*Martin Dušek,Sebastian Figura,Jakub Michal Polak,Solomon William Kamugasa,Dirk Mergelkuhl,Witold Niewiem,Štěpán Kunc,Jean-Christophe Gayde,Miroslav Šulc*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: This paper presents experimental results evaluating a straight-line reference alignment system using pseudo-nondiffracting Layer beams. Sensors with four CMOS chips and a square aperture showed high performance, with RMSE under specific thresholds, and a proof-of-concept for radiation-hard use with optical fibers is demonstrated.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is likely to advance metrology or precision systems, especially for high-radiation environments like accelerators.

Method: The method involves designing sensors, measuring beam paths without disrupting the reference, comparing with a laser tracker, and analyzing noise sources.

Result: The results show high accuracy (RMSE < 30 µm) and precision (standard deviation < 4.3 µm). Additionally, a radiation-hard sensor using optical fibers achieves even higher accuracy (RMSE < 1.3 µm).

Conclusion: The findings suggest a robust system with potential applications in radiation-prone areas such as accelerator facilities. Future developments, including addressing noise sources and improving sensor integration, are recommended.

Abstract: This paper presents experimental results that allow for the performance
evaluation of a straight-line reference alignment system based on
pseudo-nondiffracting Layer beams. Sensors, developed specifically for this
system, feature four linear CMOS chips and a square aperture. This allows for
simultaneous measurements along the beam path without disrupting the laser
reference. Measurements, conducted over a distance of 2 m from the first to the
last sensor, were compared with a laser tracker measurement to assess the
sensor performance. The alignment reference generated by the Layer Beams
exhibited a repeatability and reproducibility root-mean-square error (RMSE) of
less than 30 ${\mu}$m. The relative alignment precision for a known
displacement was validated with a standard deviation of 4.3 ${\mu}$m. The
results highlight the underlying sources of noise, which are induced mainly by
the cover glass, the protective film of the pixels, and the dark noise of the
CMOS chips. Solutions to address these challenges are proposed. Additionally, a
proof-of-concept for future development of a radiation-hard sensor utilizing
optical fiber matrices is demonstrated. The RMSE of the reference position
detection introduced by the fiber matrix remained below 1.3 ${\mu}$m. This
would allow the sensor to be used reliably in high-radiation environments
typical for accelerator facilities. This study serves as a foundational step
toward developing a robust straight-line reference alignment system based on
pseudo-nondiffracting Layer beams intended for deployment in the accelerator
facilities.

</details>

### [207] [Dark Count Rate Stability of JUNO 20-inch PMTs in Mass Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15164)
*Min Li,Narongkiat Rodphai,Caimei Liu,Zhimin Wang,Zhaoyuan Peng,Jun Wang,Nikolay Anfimov,Denis Korablev,Tobias Lachenmaier,Alexander G. Olshevskiy,Zhonghua Qin,Tobias Sterr,Alexander Felix Tietzsch,Rong Zhao,Wei Wang,Kaile Wen,Bjoern Soenke Wonsak,Wan Xie,Meihang Xu,Yu Zhang*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 文章详细分析了 Jiangmen Underground Neutrino Observatory (JUNO) 中的 20 英寸 PMT 的 dark count rate (DCR)，探讨了影响其稳定性的因素，并提出了实时监控系统。结果显示不同类型的 PMT 有显著的 DCR 差异，还发现了 DCR 爆发的初步迹象。这些研究对 JUNO 实验室的 PMT 性能优化至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度的中微子测量需要非常稳定的探测器，尤其是 PMT。PMT 的 dark count rate 不但影响到能量测量的准确性，还可能引入不可忽视的噪声。因此，深入研究 JUNO PMT 的 DCR 特性对于实验的成功运行至关重要。

Method: 文章通过 JUNO 的 20 英寸 PMT 测试设施，对单个 PMT 的 DCR 进行了详细的测量和分析，包括测量 DCR 值、稳定性和温度依赖性。同时，还比较了两种不同类型的 PMT 在 DCR 上的差异，并通过长时间的环境测试观察其稳定性。此外，运用了 Coincidence Rate Analysis 和互补成像技术，找到了 DCR 爆发的可能原因。

Result: 研究发现，两种不同类型的 PMT 在 DCR 方面存在显著差异：热量条件、温度变化和长期稳定性均对 DCR 发生影响。这些发现不仅澄清了 DCR 的成因，也为 JUNO 实验室的 PMT 后期优化和性能提升提供了重要依据。 Additionally, 初步发现 PMT 的 DCR 发生了明显的爆发，可能的原因包括闪烁器事件等。

Conclusion: 这项研究对 JUNO 实验室中使用 20 英寸 PMT 的 DCR 表征和优化具有重要意义，为后续的能量分辨率目标提供了理论支持。 此外，提出的实时 DCR 监控系统也将有助于提高 JUNO 实验的科学成功率。 通过分析 PMT 的温度依赖性以及各种环境因素，研究者们为 JUNO 的 PMT 系统开发提供了关键指导。

Abstract: The Jiangmen Underground Neutrino Observatory (JUNO) is an ambitious multipurpose neutrino experiment designed to determine the neutrino mass ordering, with an impressive energy resolution goal of at least 3% at 1 MeV. To achieve a photon detection coverage of approximately 75%, JUNO will utilize two types of 20-inch photomultiplier tubes (PMTs): the large PMT (LPMT) and the microchannel plate PMT (MCP-PMT). A significant concern in high-precision neutrino measurements is the dark count rate (DCR) of PMTs, which introduces noise that can adversely affect energy measurement accuracy. During the mass testing phase of the JUNO 20-inch PMTs, comprehensive measurements of the DCR were undertaken. These measurements not only captured the DCR values of individual PMTs but also examined the stability and temperature dependence of the DCR at an operating gain of (1x10^7). This paper presents a detailed characterization of the DCR of the JUNO 20-inch PMTs, investigating factors such as cooling time, temperature variations, and long-term stability using the JUNO Pan-Asia PMT testing facilities. The results reveal distinct DCR characteristics between the two types of PMTs, providing valuable insights into the nature of DCR and its implications for JUNO's scientific objectives. In addition to performance characterization, we implemented a monitoring system to track DCR stability over time. Notably, several spikes in DCR were identified, prompting a preliminary investigation into their causes. Potential factors contributing to these spikes, such as flasher events, were explored using coincidence rate analysis and complementary imaging techniques. The findings from this study are crucial for optimizing the performance of PMTs in JUNO, ultimately aiding the experiment in achieving its goals related to neutrino physics.

</details>
